## Job Scheduler
Libraries for scheduling jobs.

* [cdule](https://github.com/deepaksinghvi/cdule) - Job scheduler library with database support ⭐ 60
* [cheek](https://github.com/bart6114/cheek) - A simple crontab like scheduler that aims to offer a KISS approach to job scheduling. ⭐ 194
* [clockwerk](https://github.com/onatm/clockwerk) - Go package to schedule periodic jobs using a simple, fluent syntax. ⭐ 182
* [cronticker](https://github.com/krayzpipes/cronticker) - A ticker implementation to support cron schedules. ⭐ 19
* [go-cron](https://github.com/rk/go-cron) - Simple Cron library for go that can execute closures or functions at varying intervals, from once a second to once a year on a specific date and time. Primarily for web applications and long running daemons. ⭐ 238
* [go-job](https://github.com/cybergarage/go-job) - A flexible and extensible job scheduling and execution library for Go. ⭐ 0
* [go-quartz](https://github.com/reugn/go-quartz) - Simple, zero-dependency scheduling library for Go. ⭐ 1995
* [go-scheduler](https://github.com/pardnchiu/go-scheduler) - Job scheduler supporting standard cron expressions, custom descriptors, intervals, and task dependencies. ⭐ 32
* [gocron](https://github.com/go-co-op/gocron) - Easy and fluent Go job scheduling. This is an actively maintained fork of jasonlvhit/gocron. ⭐ 6895
* [goflow](https://github.com/fieldryand/goflow) - A simple but powerful DAG scheduler and dashboard. ⭐ 471
* [gron](https://github.com/roylee0704/gron) - Define time-based tasks using a simple Go API and Gron’s scheduler will run them accordingly. ⭐ 1042
* [gronx](https://github.com/adhocore/gronx) - Cron expression parser, task runner and daemon consuming crontab like task list. ⭐ 485
* [JobRunner](https://github.com/bamzi/jobrunner) - Smart and featureful cron job scheduler with job queuing and live monitoring built in. ⭐ 1087
* [leprechaun](https://github.com/kilgaloon/leprechaun) - Job scheduler that supports webhooks, crons and classic scheduling. ⭐ 106
* [sched](https://github.com/romshark/sched) - A job scheduler with the ability to fast-forward time. ⭐ 28
* [scheduler](https://github.com/carlescere/scheduler) - Cronjobs scheduling made easy. ⭐ 469
* [tasks](https://github.com/madflojo/tasks) - An easy to use in-process scheduler for recurring tasks in Go. ⭐ 321

## JSON
Libraries for working with JSON.

* [ajson](https://github.com/spyzhov/ajson) - Abstract JSON for golang with JSONPath support. ⭐ 291
* [ask](https://github.com/simonnilsson/ask) - Easy access to nested values in maps and slices. Works in combination with encoding/json and other packages that "Unmarshal" arbitrary data into Go data-types. ⭐ 56
* [dynjson](https://github.com/cocoonspace/dynjson) - Client-customizable JSON formats for dynamic APIs. ⭐ 16
* [ej](https://github.com/lucassscaravelli/ej) - Write and read JSON from different sources succinctly. ⭐ 10
* [epoch](https://github.com/vtopc/epoch) - Contains primitives for marshaling/unmarshalling Unix timestamp/epoch to/from build-in time.Time type in JSON. ⭐ 17
* [fastjson](https://github.com/valyala/fastjson) - Fast JSON parser and validator for Go. No custom structs, no code generation, no reflection. ⭐ 2429
* [gabs](https://github.com/Jeffail/gabs) - For parsing, creating and editing unknown or dynamic JSON in Go. ⭐ 3529
* [gjo](https://github.com/skanehira/gjo) - Small utility to create JSON objects. ⭐ 132
* [GJSON](https://github.com/tidwall/gjson) - Get a JSON value with one line of code. ⭐ 15437
* [go-jsonerror](https://github.com/ddymko/go-jsonerror) - Go-JsonError is meant to allow us to easily create json response errors that follow the JsonApi spec. ⭐ 16
* [go-respond](https://github.com/nicklaw5/go-respond) - Go package for handling common HTTP JSON responses. ⭐ 55
* [gojmapr](https://github.com/limiu82214/gojmapr) - Get simple struct from complex json by json path. ⭐ 22
* [gojq](https://github.com/elgs/gojq) - JSON query in Golang. ⭐ 189
* [gojson](https://github.com/ChimeraCoder/gojson) - Automatically generate Go (golang) struct definitions from example JSON. ⭐ 2694
* [htmljson](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/htmljson) - Rich rendering of JSON as HTML in Go. ⭐ 9
* [JayDiff](https://github.com/yazgazan/jaydiff) - JSON diff utility written in Go. ⭐ 110
* [jettison](https://github.com/wI2L/jettison) - Fast and flexible JSON encoder for Go. ⭐ 180
* [jscan](https://github.com/romshark/jscan) - High performance zero-allocation JSON iterator. ⭐ 99
* [JSON-to-Go](https://mholt.github.io/json-to-go/) - Convert JSON to Go struct.
* [JSON-to-Proto](https://json-to-proto.github.io/) - Convert JSON to Protobuf online.
* [json2go](https://github.com/m-zajac/json2go) - Advanced JSON to Go struct conversion. Provides package that can parse multiple JSON documents and create struct to fit them all. ⭐ 138
* [jsonapi-errors](https://github.com/AmuzaTkts/jsonapi-errors) - Go bindings based on the JSON API errors reference. ⭐ 13
* [jsoncolor](https://github.com/neilotoole/jsoncolor) - Drop-in replacement for encoding/json that outputs colorized JSON. ⭐ 49
* [jsondiff](https://github.com/wI2L/jsondiff) - JSON diff library for Go based on RFC6902 (JSON Patch). ⭐ 620
* [jsonf](https://github.com/miolini/jsonf) - Console tool for highlighted formatting and struct query fetching JSON. ⭐ 65
* [jsongo](https://github.com/ricardolonga/jsongo) - Fluent API to make it easier to create Json objects. ⭐ 108
* [jsonhal](https://github.com/RichardKnop/jsonhal) - Simple Go package to make custom structs marshal into HAL compatible JSON responses. ⭐ 13
* [jsonhandlers](https://github.com/abusomani/jsonhandlers) - JSON library to expose simple handlers that lets you easily read and write json from various sources. ⭐ 2
* [jsonic](https://github.com/sinhashubham95/jsonic) - Utilities to handle and query JSON without defining structs in a type safe manner. ⭐ 11
* [jsonvalue](https://github.com/Andrew-M-C/go.jsonvalue) - A fast and convenient library for unstructured JSON data, replacing encoding/json. ⭐ 202
* [jzon](https://github.com/zerosnake0/jzon) - JSON library with standard compatible API/behavior. ⭐ 11
* [kazaam](https://github.com/Qntfy/kazaam) - API for arbitrary transformation of JSON documents. ⭐ 292
* [mapslice-json](https://github.com/mickep76/mapslice-json) - Go MapSlice for ordered marshal/ unmarshal of maps in JSON. ⭐ 20
* [marshmallow](https://github.com/PerimeterX/marshmallow) - Performant JSON unmarshalling for flexible use cases. ⭐ 391
* [mp](https://github.com/sanbornm/mp) - Simple cli email parser. It currently takes stdin and outputs JSON. ⭐ 47
* [OjG](https://github.com/ohler55/ojg) - Optimized JSON for Go is a high performance parser with a variety of additional JSON tools including JSONPath. ⭐ 933
* [omg.jsonparser](https://github.com/dedalqq/omg.jsonparser) - Simple JSON parser with validation by condition via golang struct fields tags. ⭐ 6
* [SJSON](https://github.com/tidwall/sjson) - Set a JSON value with one line of code. ⭐ 2692
* [ujson](https://github.com/olvrng/ujson) - Fast and minimal JSON parser and transformer that works on unstructured JSON. ⭐ 85
* [vjson](https://github.com/miladibra10/vjson) - Go package for validating JSON objects with declaring a JSON schema with fluent API. ⭐ 41

## Logging
Libraries for generating and working with log files.

* [distillog](https://github.com/amoghe/distillog) - distilled levelled logging (think of it as stdlib + log levels). ⭐ 31

* [glog](https://github.com/golang/glog) - Leveled execution logs for Go. ⭐ 3617
* [go-cronowriter](https://github.com/utahta/go-cronowriter) - Simple writer that rotate log files automatically based on current date and time, like cronolog. ⭐ 57
* [go-log](https://github.com/pieterclaerhout/go-log) - A logging library with stack traces, object dumping and optional timestamps. ⭐ 11
* [go-log](https://github.com/subchen/go-log) - Simple and configurable Logging in Go, with level, formatters and writers. ⭐ 14
* [go-log](https://github.com/siddontang/go-log) - Log lib supports level and multi handlers. ⭐ 38
* [go-log](https://github.com/ian-kent/go-log) - Log4j implementation in Go. ⭐ 42
* [go-logger](https://github.com/apsdehal/go-logger) - Simple logger of Go Programs, with level handlers. ⭐ 289
* [gone/log](https://github.com/One-com/gone/tree/master/log) - Fast, extendable, full-featured, std-lib source compatible log library.
* [httpretty](https://github.com/henvic/httpretty) - Pretty-prints your regular HTTP requests on your terminal for debugging (similar to http.DumpRequest). ⭐ 413
* [journald](https://github.com/ssgreg/journald) - Go implementation of systemd Journal's native API for logging. ⭐ 46
* [kemba](https://github.com/clok/kemba) - A tiny debug logging tool inspired by debug, great for CLI tools and applications. ⭐ 17
* [lazyjournal](https://github.com/Lifailon/lazyjournal) - A TUI for reading and filtering logs from journalctl, file system, Docker and Podman containers, as well Kubernetes pods. ⭐ 1087
* [log](https://github.com/aerogo/log) - An O(1) logging system that allows you to connect one log to multiple writers (e.g. stdout, a file and a TCP connection). ⭐ 10
* [log](https://github.com/apex/log) - Structured logging package for Go. ⭐ 1377
* [log](https://github.com/go-playground/log) - Simple, configurable and scalable Structured Logging for Go. ⭐ 295
* [log](https://github.com/teris-io/log) - Structured log interface for Go cleanly separates logging facade from its implementation. ⭐ 26
* [log](https://github.com/heartwilltell/log) - Simple leveled logging wrapper around standard log package. ⭐ 17
* [log](https://github.com/no-src/log) - A simple logging framework out of the box. ⭐ 3
* [log15](https://github.com/inconshreveable/log15) - Simple, powerful logging for Go. ⭐ 1100
* [logdump](https://github.com/ewwwwwqm/logdump) - Package for multi-level logging. ⭐ 11
* [logex](https://github.com/chzyer/logex) - Golang log lib, supports tracking and level, wrap by standard log lib. ⭐ 42
* [logger](https://github.com/azer/logger) - Minimalistic logging library for Go. ⭐ 157
* [logo](https://github.com/mbndr/logo) - Golang logger to different configurable writers. ⭐ 12
* [logrus](https://github.com/Sirupsen/logrus) - Structured logger for Go. ⭐ 25683
* [logrusiowriter](https://github.com/cabify/logrusiowriter) - io.Writer implementation using logrus logger. ⭐ 16
* [logrusly](https://github.com/sebest/logrusly) - logrus plug-in to send errors to a Loggly. ⭐ 29
* [logutils](https://github.com/hashicorp/logutils) - Utilities for slightly better logging in Go (Golang) extending the standard logger. ⭐ 369
* [logxi](https://github.com/mgutz/logxi) - 12-factor app logger that is fast and makes you happy. ⭐ 360
* [lumberjack](https://github.com/natefinch/lumberjack) - Simple rolling logger, implements io.WriteCloser. ⭐ 5361
* [mlog](https://github.com/jbrodriguez/mlog) - Simple logging module for go, with 5 levels, an optional rotating logfile feature and stdout/stderr output. ⭐ 33
* [noodlog](https://github.com/gyozatech/noodlog) - Parametrized JSON logging library which lets you obfuscate sensitive data and marshal any kind of content. No more printed pointers instead of values, nor escape chars for the JSON strings. ⭐ 44
* [onelog](https://github.com/francoispqt/onelog) - Onelog is a dead simple but very efficient JSON logger. It is the fastest JSON logger out there in all scenarios. Also, it is one of the logger with the lowest allocation. ⭐ 413
* [ozzo-log](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-log) - High performance logging supporting log severity, categorization, and filtering. Can send filtered log messages to various targets (e.g. console, network, mail). ⭐ 123
* [phuslu/log](https://github.com/phuslu/log) - High performance structured logging. ⭐ 833
* [pp](https://github.com/k0kubun/pp) - Colored pretty printer for Go language. ⭐ 2027
* [rollingwriter](https://github.com/arthurkiller/rollingWriter) - RollingWriter is an auto-rotate io.Writer implementation with multi policies to provide log file rotation. ⭐ 295
* [seelog](https://github.com/cihub/seelog) - Logging functionality with flexible dispatching, filtering, and formatting. ⭐ 1640
* [sentry-go](https://github.com/getsentry/sentry-go) - Sentry SDK for Go. Helps monitor and track errors with real-time alerts and performance monitoring. ⭐ 1037
* [slf4g](https://github.com/echocat/slf4g) - Simple Logging Facade for Golang: Simple structured logging; but powerful, extendable and customizable, with huge amount of learnings from decades of past logging frameworks. ⭐ 5
* [slog](https://github.com/gookit/slog) - Lightweight, configurable, extensible logger for Go. ⭐ 533
* [slog-formatter](https://github.com/samber/slog-formatter) - Common formatters for slog and helpers to build your own. ⭐ 209
* [slog-multi](https://github.com/samber/slog-multi) - Chain of slog.Handler (pipeline, fanout...). ⭐ 604
* [slogor](https://gitlab.com/greyxor/slogor) - A colorful slog handler. ⭐ 19
* [spew](https://github.com/davecgh/go-spew) - Implements a deep pretty printer for Go data structures to aid in debugging. ⭐ 6367
* [sqldb-logger](https://github.com/simukti/sqldb-logger) - A logger for Go SQL database driver without modify existing *sql.DB stdlib usage. ⭐ 383
* [stdlog](https://github.com/alexcesaro/log) - Stdlog is an object-oriented library providing leveled logging. It is very useful for cron jobs. ⭐ 48
* [structy/log](https://github.com/structy/log) - A simple to use log system, minimalist but with features for debugging and differentiation of messages. ⭐ 5
* [tail](https://github.com/hpcloud/tail) - Go package striving to emulate the features of the BSD tail program. ⭐ 2779
* [timberjack](https://github.com/DeRuina/timberjack) - Rolling logger with size-based, time-based, and scheduled clock-based rotation, supporting compression and cleanup. ⭐ 114
* [tint](https://github.com/lmittmann/tint) - A slog.Handler that writes tinted logs. ⭐ 1211
* [xlog](https://github.com/xfxdev/xlog) - Plugin architecture and flexible log system for Go, with level ctrl, multiple log target and custom log format. ⭐ 8
* [xlog](https://github.com/rs/xlog) - Structured logger for net/context aware HTTP handlers with flexible dispatching. ⭐ 141
* [xylog](https://github.com/xybor-x/xylog) - Leveled and structured logging, dynamic fields, high performance, zone management, simple configuration, and readable syntax. ⭐ 17
* [yell](https://github.com/jfcg/yell) - Yet another minimalistic logging library. ⭐ 1
* [zap](https://github.com/uber-go/zap) - Fast, structured, leveled logging in Go. ⭐ 24199
* [zax](https://github.com/yuseferi/zax) - Integrate Context with Zap logger, which leads to more flexibility in Go logging. ⭐ 32
* [zerolog](https://github.com/rs/zerolog) - Zero-allocation JSON logger. ⭐ 12172
* [zkits-logger](https://github.com/edoger/zkits-logger) - A powerful zero-dependency JSON logger. ⭐ 28

* [ami](https://github.com/kak-tus/ami) - Go client to reliable queues based on Redis Cluster Streams. ⭐ 34

* [Asynq](https://github.com/hibiken/asynq) - A simple, reliable, and efficient distributed task queue for Go built on top of Redis. ⭐ 12840

* [Beaver](https://github.com/Clivern/Beaver) - A real time messaging server to build a scalable in-app notifications, multiplayer games, chat apps in web and mobile apps. ⭐ 1583
* [Bus](https://github.com/mustafaturan/bus) - Minimalist message bus implementation for internal communication. ⭐ 359
* [Centrifugo](https://github.com/centrifugal/centrifugo) - Real-time messaging (Websockets or SockJS) server in Go. ⭐ 9901
* [Chanify](https://github.com/chanify/chanify) - A push notification server send message to your iOS devices. ⭐ 1322
* [Commander](https://github.com/jeroenrinzema/commander) - A high-level event driven consumer/producer supporting various "dialects" such as Apache Kafka. ⭐ 67
* [Confluent Kafka Golang Client](https://github.com/confluentinc/confluent-kafka-go) - confluent-kafka-go is Confluent's Golang client for Apache Kafka and the Confluent Platform. ⭐ 5098
* [dbus](https://github.com/godbus/dbus) - Native Go bindings for D-Bus. ⭐ 1138
* [drone-line](https://github.com/appleboy/drone-line) - Sending Line notifications using a binary, docker or Drone CI. ⭐ 80
* [emitter](https://github.com/olebedev/emitter) - Emits events using Go way, with wildcard, predicates, cancellation possibilities and many other good wins. ⭐ 525
* [event](https://github.com/agoalofalife/event) - Implementation of the pattern observer. ⭐ 62
* [EventBus](https://github.com/asaskevich/EventBus) - The lightweight event bus with async compatibility. ⭐ 1954
* [gaurun-client](https://github.com/osamingo/gaurun-client) - Gaurun Client written in Go. ⭐ 11
* [Glue](https://github.com/desertbit/glue) - Robust Go and Javascript Socket Library (Alternative to Socket.io). ⭐ 421
* [go-eventbus](https://github.com/stanipetrosyan/go-eventbus) - Simple Event Bus package for Go. ⭐ 9
* [Go-MediatR](https://github.com/mehdihadeli/Go-MediatR) - A library for handling mediator patterns and simplified CQRS patterns within an event-driven architecture, inspired by csharp MediatR library. ⭐ 274
* [go-mq](https://github.com/cheshir/go-mq) - RabbitMQ client with declarative configuration. ⭐ 91
* [go-notify](https://github.com/TheCreeper/go-notify) - Native implementation of the freedesktop notification spec. ⭐ 71
* [go-nsq](https://github.com/nsqio/go-nsq) - the official Go package for NSQ. ⭐ 2661
* [go-res](https://github.com/jirenius/go-res) - Package for building REST/real-time services where clients are synchronized seamlessly, using NATS and Resgate. ⭐ 67
* [go-vitotrol](https://github.com/maxatome/go-vitotrol) - Client library to Viessmann Vitotrol web service. ⭐ 23
* [GoEventBus](https://github.com/Raezil/GoEventBus) - A blazing‑fast, in‑memory, lock‑free event bus library ⭐ 53
* [Gollum](https://github.com/trivago/gollum) - A n:m multiplexer that gathers messages from different sources and broadcasts them to a set of destinations. ⭐ 940
* [golongpoll](https://github.com/jcuga/golongpoll) - HTTP longpoll server library that makes web pub-sub simple. ⭐ 666
* [gopush-cluster](https://github.com/Terry-Mao/gopush-cluster) - gopush-cluster is a go push server cluster. ⭐ 2075
* [gorush](https://github.com/appleboy/gorush) - Push notification server using APNs2 and google GCM. ⭐ 8681
* [gosd](https://github.com/alexsniffin/gosd) - A library for scheduling when to dispatch a message to a channel. ⭐ 26
* [guble](https://github.com/smancke/guble) - Messaging server using push notifications (Google Firebase Cloud Messaging, Apple Push Notification services, SMS) as well as websockets, a REST API, featuring distributed operation and message-persistence. ⭐ 161
* [hare](https://github.com/leozz37/hare) - A user friendly library for sending messages and listening to TCP sockets. ⭐ 54
* [hub](https://github.com/leandro-lugaresi/hub) - A Message/Event Hub for Go applications, using publish/subscribe pattern with support for alias like rabbitMQ exchanges. ⭐ 149
* [hypermatch](https://github.com/SchwarzIT/hypermatch) - A very fast and efficient Go library for matching events to a large set of rules ⭐ 33
* [jazz](https://github.com/socifi/jazz) - A simple RabbitMQ abstraction layer for queue administration and publishing and consuming of messages. ⭐ 18
* [machinery](https://github.com/RichardKnop/machinery) - Asynchronous task queue/job queue based on distributed message passing. ⭐ 7944
* [mangos](https://github.com/nanomsg/mangos) - Pure go implementation of the Nanomsg ("Scalability Protocols") with transport interoperability. ⭐ 743
* [melody](https://github.com/olahol/melody) - Minimalist framework for dealing with websocket sessions, includes broadcasting and automatic ping/pong handling. ⭐ 4059
* [Mercure](https://github.com/dunglas/mercure) - Server and library to dispatch server-sent updates using the Mercure protocol (built on top of Server-Sent Events). ⭐ 5175
* [messagebus](https://github.com/vardius/message-bus) - messagebus is a Go simple async message bus, perfect for using as event bus when doing event sourcing, CQRS, DDD. ⭐ 286
* [NATS Go Client](https://github.com/nats-io/nats.go) - Go client for the NATS
messaging system. ⭐ 6415
* [nsq-event-bus](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/nsq-event-bus) - A tiny wrapper around NSQ topic and channel. ⭐ 80
* [oplog](https://github.com/dailymotion/oplog) - Generic oplog/replication system for REST APIs. ⭐ 110
* [pubsub](https://github.com/tuxychandru/pubsub) - Simple pubsub package for go. ⭐ 447
* [Quamina](https://github.com/timbray/quamina) - Fast pattern-matching for filtering messages and events. ⭐ 474
* [rabbitroutine](https://github.com/furdarius/rabbitroutine) - Lightweight library that handles RabbitMQ auto-reconnect and publishing retries. The library takes into account the need to re-declare entities in RabbitMQ after reconnection. ⭐ 114
* [rabbus](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/rabbus) - A tiny wrapper over amqp exchanges and queues. ⭐ 98
* [rabtap](https://github.com/jandelgado/rabtap) - RabbitMQ swiss army knife cli app. ⭐ 278
* [RapidMQ](https://github.com/sybrexsys/RapidMQ) - RapidMQ is a lightweight and reliable library for managing of the local messages queue. ⭐ 70
* [Ratus](https://github.com/hyperonym/ratus) - Ratus is a RESTful asynchronous task queue server. ⭐ 124
* [redisqueue](https://github.com/robinjoseph08/redisqueue) - redisqueue provides a producer and consumer of a queue that uses Redis streams. ⭐ 139
* [rmqconn](https://github.com/sbabiv/rmqconn) - RabbitMQ Reconnection. Wrapper over amqp.Connection and amqp.Dial. Allowing to do a reconnection when the connection is broken before forcing the call to the Close () method to be closed. ⭐ 23
* [sarama](https://github.com/Shopify/sarama) - Go library for Apache Kafka. ⭐ 12416
* [Uniqush-Push](https://github.com/uniqush/uniqush-push) - Redis backed unified push service for server-side notifications to mobile devices. ⭐ 1562
* [varmq](https://github.com/goptics/varmq) - A storage-agnostic message queue and worker pool for concurrent Go programs. ⭐ 176
* [Watermill](https://github.com/ThreeDotsLabs/watermill) - Working efficiently with message streams. Building event driven applications, enabling event sourcing, RPC over messages, sagas. Can use conventional pub/sub implementations like Kafka or RabbitMQ, but also HTTP or MySQL binlog. ⭐ 9482
* [zmq4](https://github.com/pebbe/zmq4) - Go interface to ZeroMQ version 4. Also available for version 3 and version 2. ⭐ 1245

## Miscellaneous
### Dependency Injection
Libraries for working with dependency injection.

* [alice](https://github.com/magic003/alice) - Additive dependency injection container for Golang. (51)
* [autowire](https://github.com/tiendc/autowire) - Dependency injection using Generics and reflection. (12)
* [boot-go](http://github.com/boot-go/boot) - Component-based development with dependency injection using reflections for Go developers. (36)
* [componego](https://github.com/componego/componego) - A dependency injection framework based on components, allowing dynamic dependency replacement without duplicating code in tests. (28)
* [cosban/di](https://gitlab.com/cosban/di) - A code generation based dependency injection wiring tool. (1)
* [di](https://github.com/goava/di) - A dependency injection container for go programming language. (240)
* [dig](https://github.com/uber-go/dig) - A reflection based dependency injection toolkit for Go. (4434)
* [dingo](https://github.com/i-love-flamingo/dingo) - A dependency injection toolkit for Go, based on Guice. (188)
* [do](https://github.com/samber/do) - A dependency injection framework based on Generics. (2623)
* [fx](https://github.com/uber-go/fx) - A dependency injection based application framework for Go (built on top of dig). (7324)
* [Go-Spring](https://github.com/go-spring/spring-core) - A high-performance Go framework inspired by Spring Boot, offering DI, auto-configuration, and lifecycle management while maintaining Go's simplicity and efficiency. (75)
* [gocontainer](https://github.com/vardius/gocontainer) - Simple Dependency Injection Container. (22)
* [godi](https://github.com/junioryono/godi) - Microsoft-style dependency injection for Go with scoped lifetimes and generics. (68)
* [goioc/di](https://github.com/goioc/di) - Spring-inspired Dependency Injection Container. (377)
* [GoLobby/Container](https://github.com/golobby/container) - GoLobby Container is a lightweight yet powerful IoC dependency injection container for the Go programming language. (611)
* [gontainer](https://github.com/NVIDIA/gontainer) - A dependency injection service container for Go projects. (63)
* [gontainer/gontainer](https://github.com/gontainer/gontainer) - A YAML-based Dependency Injection container for GO. It supports dependencies' scopes, and auto-detection of circular dependencies. Gontainer is concurrent-safe. (16)
* [HnH/di](https://github.com/HnH/di) - DI container library that is focused on clean API and flexibility. (8)
* [kinit](https://github.com/go-kata/kinit) - Customizable dependency injection container with the global mode, cascade initialization and panic-safe finalization. (10)
* [kod](https://github.com/go-kod/kod) - A generics based dependency injection framework for Go. (196)
* [linker](https://github.com/logrange/linker) - A reflection based dependency injection and inversion of control library with components lifecycle support. (35)
* [nject](https://github.com/muir/nject) - A type safe, reflective framework for libraries, tests, http endpoints, and service startup. (30)
* [ore](https://github.com/firasdarwish/ore) - Lightweight, generic & simple dependency injection (DI) container. (24)
* [parsley](https://github.com/matzefriedrich/parsley) - A flexible and modular reflection-based DI library with advanced features like scoped contexts and proxy generation, designed for large-scale Go applications. (30)
* [wire](https://github.com/Fs02/wire) - Strict Runtime Dependency Injection for Golang. (40)
### Project Layout

* [ardanlabs/service](https://github.com/ardanlabs/service) - A starter kit for building production grade scalable web service applications. (3928)

* [go-module](https://github.com/octomation/go-module) - Template for a typical module written on Go. (36)
* [go-sample](https://github.com/zitryss/go-sample) - A sample layout for Go application projects with the real code. (137)
* [go-starter](https://github.com/allaboutapps/go-starter) - An opinionated production-ready RESTful JSON backend template, highly integrated with VSCode DevContainers. (593)
* [go-todo-backend](https://github.com/Fs02/go-todo-backend) - Go Todo Backend example using modular project layout for product microservice. (335)
* [goapp](https://github.com/naughtygopher/goapp) - An opinionated guideline to structure & develop a Go web application/service. (1048)
* [gobase](https://github.com/wajox/gobase) - A simple skeleton for golang application with basic setup for real golang application. (66)
* [golang-standards/project-layout](https://github.com/golang-standards/project-layout) - Set of common historical and emerging project layout patterns in the Go ecosystem. Note: despite the org-name they do not represent official golang standards, see this issue for more information. Nonetheless, some may find the layout useful. (55261)
* [golang-templates/seed](https://github.com/golang-templates/seed) - Go application GitHub repository template. (553)
* [goxygen](https://github.com/shpota/goxygen) - Generate a modern Web project with Go and Angular, React, or Vue in seconds. (3604)
* [insidieux/inizio](https://github.com/insidieux/inizio) - Golang project layout generator with plugins. (18)
* [kickstart.go](https://github.com/raeperd/kickstart.go) - Minimalistic single-file Go HTTP server template without third-party dependencies. (102)

* [nunu](https://github.com/go-nunu/nunu) - Nunu is a scaffolding tool for building Go applications. (2539)
* [pagoda](https://github.com/mikestefanello/pagoda) - Rapid, easy full-stack web development starter kit built in Go. (2904)
* [scaffold](https://github.com/catchplay/scaffold) - Scaffold generates a starter Go project layout. Lets you focus on business logic implemented. (148)

## Natural Language Processing
See also Text Processing and Text Analysis.
### Language Detection

* [detectlanguage](https://github.com/detectlanguage/detectlanguage-go) - Language Detection API Go Client. Supports batch requests, short phrase or single word language detection. (26)
* [getlang](https://github.com/rylans/getlang) - Fast natural language detection package. (175)
* [guesslanguage](https://github.com/endeveit/guesslanguage) - Functions to determine the natural language of a unicode text. (58)
* [lingua-go](https://github.com/pemistahl/lingua-go) - An accurate natural language detection library, suitable for long and short text alike. Supports detecting multiple languages in mixed-language text. (1317)
* [whatlanggo](https://github.com/abadojack/whatlanggo) - Natural language detection package for Go. Supports 84 languages and 24 scripts (writing systems e.g. Latin, Cyrillic, etc). (680)
### Morphological Analyzers

* [go-stem](https://github.com/agonopol/go-stem) - Implementation of the porter stemming algorithm. (82)
* [go2vec](https://github.com/danieldk/go2vec) - Reader and utility functions for word2vec embeddings. (58)
* [golibstemmer](https://github.com/rjohnsondev/golibstemmer) - Go bindings for the snowball libstemmer library including porter 2. (21)
* [gosentiwordnet](https://github.com/dinopuguh/gosentiwordnet) - Sentiment analyzer using sentiwordnet lexicon in Go. (11)
* [govader](https://github.com/jonreiter/govader) - Go implementation of VADER Sentiment Analysis. (52)
* [govader-backend](https://github.com/PIMPfiction/govader_backend) - Microservice implementation of GoVader. (7)
* [kagome](https://github.com/ikawaha/kagome) - JP morphological analyzer written in pure Go. (940)
* [libtextcat](https://github.com/goodsign/libtextcat) - Cgo binding for libtextcat C library. Guaranteed compatibility with version 2.2. (13)
* [nlp](https://github.com/james-bowman/nlp) - Go Natural Language Processing library supporting LSA (Latent Semantic Analysis). (467)
* [paicehusk](https://github.com/rookii/paicehusk) - Golang implementation of the Paice/Husk Stemming Algorithm. (29)
* [porter](https://github.com/a2800276/porter) - This is a fairly straightforward port of Martin Porter's C implementation of the Porter stemming algorithm. (12)
* [porter2](https://github.com/zhenjl/porter2) - Really fast Porter 2 stemmer. (47)
* [RAKE.go](https://github.com/afjoseph/RAKE.Go) - Go port of the Rapid Automatic Keyword Extraction Algorithm (RAKE). (122)
* [snowball](https://github.com/goodsign/snowball) - Snowball stemmer port (cgo wrapper) for Go. Provides word stem extraction functionality Snowball native. (38)
* [spaGO](https://github.com/nlpodyssey/spago) - Self-contained Machine Learning and Natural Language Processing library in Go. (1842)
* [spelling-corrector](https://github.com/jorelosorio/spellingcorrector) - A spelling corrector for the Spanish language or create your own. (2)
### Slugifiers

* [go-slugify](https://github.com/mozillazg/go-slugify) - Make pretty slug with multiple languages support. (97)
* [slug](https://github.com/gosimple/slug) - URL-friendly slugify with multiple languages support. (1316)
* [Slugify](https://github.com/avelino/slugify) - Go slugify application that handles string. (35)
### Tokenizers

* [gojieba](https://github.com/yanyiwu/gojieba) - This is a Go implementation of jieba which a Chinese word splitting algorithm. (2618)
* [gotokenizer](https://github.com/xujiajun/gotokenizer) - A tokenizer based on the dictionary and Bigram language models for Golang. (Now only support chinese segmentation) (21)
* [gse](https://github.com/go-ego/gse) - Go efficient text segmentation; support english, chinese, japanese and other. (2778)
* [MMSEGO](https://github.com/awsong/MMSEGO) - This is a GO implementation of MMSEG which a Chinese word splitting algorithm. (62)
* [segment](https://github.com/blevesearch/segment) - Go library for performing Unicode Text Segmentation as described in Unicode Standard Annex #29 (88)
* [sentences](https://github.com/neurosnap/sentences) - Sentence tokenizer: converts text into a list of sentences. (463)
* [shamoji](https://github.com/osamingo/shamoji) - The shamoji is word filtering package written in Go. (13)
* [stemmer](https://github.com/dchest/stemmer) - Stemmer packages for Go programming language. Includes English and German stemmers. (54)
* [textcat](https://github.com/pebbe/textcat) - Go package for n-gram based text categorization, with support for utf-8 and raw text. (73)
### Translation

* [ctxi18n](https://github.com/invopop/ctxi18n/) - Context aware i18n with a short and consise API, pluralization, interpolation, and fs.FS support. YAML locale definitions are based on Rails i18n. (92)
* [go-i18n](https://github.com/nicksnyder/go-i18n/) - Package and an accompanying tool to work with localized text. (3461)
* [go-mystem](https://github.com/dveselov/mystem) - CGo bindings to Yandex.Mystem - russian morphology analyzer. (35)
* [go-pinyin](https://github.com/mozillazg/go-pinyin) - CN Hanzi to Hanyu Pinyin converter. (1755)
* [go-words](https://github.com/saleh-rahimzadeh/go-words) - A words table and text resource library for Golang projects. (8)
* [gotext](https://github.com/leonelquinteros/gotext) - GNU gettext utilities for Go. (489)
* [iuliia-go](https://github.com/mehanizm/iuliia-go) - Transliterate Cyrillic → Latin in every possible way. (56)
* [spreak](https://github.com/vorlif/spreak) - Flexible translation and humanization library for Go, based on the concepts behind gettext. (92)
* [t](https://github.com/youthlin/t) - Another i18n pkg for golang, which follows GNU gettext style and supports .po/.mo files: t.T (gettext), t.N (ngettext), etc. And it contains a cmd tool xtemplate, which can extract messages as a pot file from text/html template. (21)
### Transliteration

* [enca](https://github.com/endeveit/enca) - Minimal cgo bindings for libenca, which detects character encodings. (19)
* [go-unidecode](https://github.com/mozillazg/go-unidecode) - ASCII transliterations of Unicode text. (144)
* [gounidecode](https://github.com/fiam/gounidecode) - Unicode transliterator (also known as unidecode) for Go. (80)
* [transliterator](https://github.com/alexsergivan/transliterator) - Provides one-way string transliteration with supporting of language-specific transliteration rules. (46)

## Networking
Libraries for working with various layers of the network.

* [arp](https://github.com/mdlayher/arp) - Package arp implements the ARP protocol, as described in RFC 826. ⭐ 381
* [bart](https://github.com/gaissmai/bart) - Package bart provides a Balanced-Routing-Table (BART) for very fast IP to CIDR lookups and more. ⭐ 116
* [buffstreams](https://github.com/stabbycutyou/buffstreams) - Streaming protocolbuffer data over TCP made easy. ⭐ 255
* [canopus](https://github.com/zubairhamed/canopus) - CoAP Client/Server implementation (RFC 7252). ⭐ 156
* [cidranger](https://github.com/yl2chen/cidranger) - Fast IP to CIDR lookup for Go. ⭐ 967
* [cloudflared](https://github.com/cloudflare/cloudflared) - Cloudflare Tunnel client (formerly Argo Tunnel). ⭐ 12891
* [dhcp6](https://github.com/mdlayher/dhcp6) - Package dhcp6 implements a DHCPv6 server, as described in RFC 3315. ⭐ 79
* [dns](https://github.com/miekg/dns) - Go library for working with DNS. ⭐ 8627
* [dnsmonster](https://github.com/mosajjal/dnsmonster) - Passive DNS Capture/Monitoring Framework. ⭐ 350
* [easytcp](https://github.com/DarthPestilane/easytcp) - A light-weight TCP framework written in Go (Golang), built with message router. EasyTCP helps you build a TCP server easily fast and less painful. ⭐ 824
* [ether](https://github.com/songgao/ether) - Cross-platform Go package for sending and receiving ethernet frames. ⭐ 81
* [ethernet](https://github.com/mdlayher/ethernet) - Package ethernet implements marshaling and unmarshalling of IEEE 802.3 Ethernet II frames and IEEE 802.1Q VLAN tags. ⭐ 284
* [event](https://github.com/cheng-zhongliang/event) - Simple I/O event notification library written in Golang. ⭐ 119
* [fasthttp](https://github.com/valyala/fasthttp) - Package fasthttp is a fast HTTP implementation for Go, up to 10 times faster than net/http. ⭐ 23243
* [fortio](https://github.com/fortio/fortio) - Load testing library and command line tool, advanced echo server and web UI. Allows to specify a set query-per-second load and record latency histograms and other useful stats and graph them. Tcp, Http, gRPC. ⭐ 3665
* [ftp](https://github.com/jlaffaye/ftp) - Package ftp implements a FTP client as described in RFC 959. ⭐ 1382
* [ftpserverlib](https://github.com/fclairamb/ftpserverlib) - Fully featured FTP server library. ⭐ 462
* [fullproxy](https://github.com/shoriwe/fullproxy) - A fully featured scriptable and daemon configurable proxy and pivoting toolkit with SOCKS5, HTTP, raw ports and reverse proxy protocols. ⭐ 82
* [fwdctl](https://github.com/alegrey91/fwdctl) - A simple and intuitive CLI to manage IPTables forwards in your Linux server. ⭐ 72
* [gaio](https://github.com/xtaci/gaio) - High performance async-io networking for Golang in proactor mode. ⭐ 1034
* [gev](https://github.com/Allenxuxu/gev) - gev is a lightweight, fast non-blocking TCP network library based on Reactor mode. ⭐ 1774
* [gldap](https://github.com/jimlambrt/gldap) - gldap provides an ldap server implementation and you provide handlers for its ldap operations. ⭐ 118
* [gmqtt](https://github.com/DrmagicE/gmqtt) - Gmqtt is a flexible, high-performance MQTT broker library that fully implements the MQTT protocol V3.1.1. ⭐ 1032
* [gnet](https://github.com/panjf2000/gnet) - gnet is a high-performance, lightweight, non-blocking, event-driven networking framework written in pure Go. ⭐ 11069
* [gnet](https://github.com/fish-tennis/gnet) - gnet is a high-performance networking framework,especially for game servers. ⭐ 26
* [gNxI](https://github.com/google/gnxi) - A collection of tools for Network Management that use the gNMI and gNOI protocols. ⭐ 283
* [go-getter](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-getter) - Go library for downloading files or directories from various sources using a URL. ⭐ 1791
* [go-multiproxy](https://github.com/presbrey/go-multiproxy) - Library for making HTTP requests through a pool of proxies offering fault tolerance, load balancing, automatic retries, cookie management, and more, via http.Get/Post replacement or http.Client RoundTripper drop-in ⭐ 28
* [go-pcaplite](https://github.com/alexcfv/go-pcaplite) - Lightweight live packet capture library with HTTPS SNI extraction. ⭐ 7
* [go-powerdns](https://github.com/joeig/go-powerdns) - PowerDNS API bindings for Golang. ⭐ 103
* [go-sse](https://github.com/lampctl/go-sse) - Go client and server implementation of HTML server-sent events. ⭐ 15
* [go-stun](https://github.com/ccding/go-stun) - Go implementation of the STUN client (RFC 3489 and RFC 5389). ⭐ 718
* [gobgp](https://github.com/osrg/gobgp) - BGP implemented in the Go Programming Language. ⭐ 3977
* [gopacket](https://github.com/google/gopacket) - Go library for packet processing with libpcap bindings. ⭐ 6732
* [gopcap](https://github.com/akrennmair/gopcap) - Go wrapper for libpcap. ⭐ 491
* [GoProxy](https://github.com/elazarl/goproxy) - A library to create a customized HTTP/HTTPS proxy server using Go. ⭐ 6587
* [goshark](https://github.com/sunwxg/goshark) - Package goshark use tshark to decode IP packet and create data struct to analyse packet. ⭐ 18
* [gosnmp](https://github.com/soniah/gosnmp) - Native Go library for performing SNMP actions. ⭐ 1235
* [gotcp](https://github.com/gansidui/gotcp) - Go package for quickly writing tcp applications. ⭐ 513
* [grab](https://github.com/cavaliercoder/grab) - Go package for managing file downloads. ⭐ 1469
* [graval](https://github.com/koofr/graval) - Experimental FTP server framework. ⭐ 28
* [gws](https://github.com/lxzan/gws) - High-Performance WebSocket Server & Client With AsyncIO Supporting . ⭐ 1702
* [HTTPLab](https://github.com/gchaincl/httplab) - HTTPLabs let you inspect HTTP requests and forge responses. ⭐ 4210
* [httpproxy](https://github.com/wzshiming/httpproxy) - HTTP proxy handler and dialer. ⭐ 32
* [iplib](https://github.com/c-robinson/iplib) - Library for working with IP addresses (net.IP, net.IPNet), inspired by python ipaddress and ruby ipaddr ⭐ 152
* [jazigo](https://github.com/udhos/jazigo) - Jazigo is a tool written in Go for retrieving configuration for multiple network devices. ⭐ 229
* [kcp-go](https://github.com/xtaci/kcp-go) - KCP - Fast and Reliable ARQ Protocol. ⭐ 4477
* [kcptun](https://github.com/xtaci/kcptun) - Extremely simple & fast udp tunnel based on KCP protocol. ⭐ 14526
* [lhttp](https://github.com/fanux/lhttp) - Powerful websocket framework, build your IM server more easily. ⭐ 690
* [linkio](https://github.com/ian-kent/linkio) - Network link speed simulation for Reader/Writer interfaces. ⭐ 55
* [llb](https://github.com/kirillDanshin/llb) - It's a very simple but quick backend for proxy servers. Can be useful for fast redirection to predefined domain with zero memory allocation and fast response. ⭐ 16
* [mdns](https://github.com/hashicorp/mdns) - Simple mDNS (Multicast DNS) client/server library in Golang. ⭐ 1331
* [mqttPaho](https://eclipse.org/paho/clients/golang/) - The Paho Go Client provides an MQTT client library for connection to MQTT brokers via TCP, TLS or WebSockets.
* [natiu-mqtt](https://github.com/soypat/natiu-mqtt) - A dead-simple, non-allocating, low level implementation of MQTT well suited for embedded systems. ⭐ 102
* [nbio](https://github.com/lesismal/nbio) - Pure Go 1000k+ connections solution, support tls/http1.x/websocket and basically compatible with net/http, with high-performance and low memory cost, non-blocking, event-driven, easy-to-use. ⭐ 2692
* [net](https://golang.org/x/net) - This repository holds supplementary Go networking libraries.
* [netpoll](https://github.com/cloudwego/netpoll) - A high-performance non-blocking I/O networking framework, which focused on RPC scenarios, developed by ByteDance. ⭐ 4529
* [NFF-Go](https://github.com/intel-go/nff-go) - Framework for rapid development of performant network functions for cloud and bare-metal (former YANFF). ⭐ 1418
* [nodepass](https://github.com/NodePassProject/nodepass) - A secure, efficient TCP/UDP tunneling solution that delivers fast, reliable access across network restrictions using pre-established TCP/QUIC/WebSocket or HTTP/2 connections. ⭐ 2023
* [peerdiscovery](https://github.com/schollz/peerdiscovery) - Pure Go library for cross-platform local peer discovery using UDP multicast. ⭐ 668
* [portproxy](https://github.com/aybabtme/portproxy) - Simple TCP proxy which adds CORS support to API's which don't support it. ⭐ 58
* [psql-wire](https://github.com/jeroenrinzema/psql-wire) - PostgreSQL server wire protocol. Build your own server and start serving connections.. ⭐ 216
* [publicip](https://github.com/polera/publicip) - Package publicip returns your public facing IPv4 address (internet egress). ⭐ 29
* [quic-go](https://github.com/lucas-clemente/quic-go) - An implementation of the QUIC protocol in pure Go. ⭐ 11381
* [sdns](https://github.com/semihalev/sdns) - A high-performance, recursive DNS resolver server with DNSSEC support, focused on preserving privacy. ⭐ 1025
* [sftp](https://github.com/pkg/sftp) - Package sftp implements the SSH File Transfer Protocol as described in https://filezilla-project.org/specs/draft-ietf-secsh-filexfer-02.txt. ⭐ 1634
* [ssh](https://github.com/gliderlabs/ssh) - Higher-level API for building SSH servers (wraps crypto/ssh). ⭐ 4082
* [sslb](https://github.com/eduardonunesp/sslb) - It's a Super Simples Load Balancer, just a little project to achieve some kind of performance. ⭐ 151
* [stun](https://github.com/go-rtc/stun) - Go implementation of RFC 5389 STUN protocol. ⭐ 496
* [tcpack](https://github.com/lim-yoona/tcpack) - tcpack is an application protocol based on TCP to Pack and Unpack bytes stream in go program. ⭐ 167
* [tspool](https://github.com/two/tspool) - A TCP Library use worker pool to improve performance and protect your server. ⭐ 14
* [tun2socks](https://github.com/xjasonlyu/tun2socks) - A pure go implementation of tun2socks powered by gVisor TCP/IP stack. ⭐ 4854
* [utp](https://github.com/anacrolix/utp) - Go uTP micro transport protocol implementation. ⭐ 182
* [vssh](https://github.com/yahoo/vssh) - Go library for building network and server automation over SSH protocol. ⭐ 991
* [water](https://github.com/songgao/water) - Simple TUN/TAP library. ⭐ 2128
* [webrtc](https://github.com/pions/webrtc) - A pure Go implementation of the WebRTC API. ⭐ 15989
* [winrm](https://github.com/masterzen/winrm) - Go WinRM client to remotely execute commands on Windows machines. ⭐ 458
* [xtcp](https://github.com/xfxdev/xtcp) - TCP Server Framework with simultaneous full duplex communication, graceful shutdown, and custom protocol. ⭐ 159
### HTTP Clients
Libraries for making HTTP requests.

* [axios4go](https://github.com/rezmoss/axios4go) - A Go HTTP client library inspired by Axios, providing a simple and intuitive API for making HTTP requests. (30)
* [azuretls-client](https://github.com/Noooste/azuretls-client) - An easy-to-use HTTP client 100% in Go to spoof TLS/JA3 and HTTP2 fingerprint. (416)
* [fast-shot](https://github.com/opus-domini/fast-shot) - Hit your API targets with rapid-fire precision using Go's fastest and simple HTTP Client. (94)
* [gentleman](https://github.com/h2non/gentleman) - Full-featured plugin-driven HTTP client library. (1124)
* [go-cleanhttp](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-cleanhttp) - Get easily stdlib HTTP client, which does not share any state with other clients. (429)
* [go-http-client](https://github.com/bozd4g/go-http-client) - Make http calls simply and easily. (85)
* [go-ipmux](https://github.com/optimus-hft/go-ipmux) - A library for Multiplexing HTTP requests based on multiple Source IPs. (28)
* [go-otelroundtripper](https://github.com/NdoleStudio/go-otelroundtripper) - Go http.RoundTripper that emits open telemetry metrics for HTTP requests. (85)
* [go-req](https://github.com/wenerme/go-req) - Declarative golang HTTP client. (23)
* [go-retryablehttp](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-retryablehttp) - Retryable HTTP client in Go. (2270)
* [go-zoox/fetch](https://github.com/go-zoox/fetch) - A Powerful, Lightweight, Easy Http Client, inspired by Web Fetch API. (89)
* [Grequest](https://github.com/lib4u/grequest) - Simple and lightweight golang package for http requests. based on powerful net/http (9)
* [grequests](https://github.com/levigross/grequests) - A Go "clone" of the great and famous Requests library. (2185)
* [heimdall](https://github.com/gojektech/heimdall) - An enhanced http client with retry and hystrix capabilities. (2699)
* [httpretry](https://github.com/ybbus/httpretry) - Enriches the default go HTTP client with retry functionality. (57)
* [pester](https://github.com/sethgrid/pester) - Go HTTP client calls with retries, backoff, and concurrency. (654)
* [req](https://github.com/imroc/req) - Simple Go HTTP client with Black Magic (Less code and More efficiency). (4754)
* [request](https://github.com/monaco-io/request) - HTTP client for golang. If you have experience about axios or requests, you will love it. No 3rd dependency. (295)
* [requests](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/requests) - HTTP requests for Gophers. Uses context.Context and doesn't hide the underlying net/http.Client, making it compatible with standard Go APIs. Also includes testing tools. (1663)
* [resty](https://github.com/go-resty/resty) - Simple HTTP and REST client for Go inspired by Ruby rest-client. (11515)
* [rq](https://github.com/ddo/rq) - A nicer interface for golang stdlib HTTP client. (53)
* [sling](https://github.com/dghubble/sling) - Sling is a Go HTTP client library for creating and sending API requests. (1717)
* [surf](https://github.com/enetx/surf) - Advanced HTTP client with HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, HTTP/3 (QUIC), SOCKS5 proxy support and browser-grade TLS fingerprinting. (1294)
* [tls-client](https://github.com/bogdanfinn/tls-client) - net/http.Client like HTTP Client with options to select specific client TLS Fingerprints to use for requests. (1431)

## ORM
Libraries that implement Object-Relational Mapping or datamapping techniques.

* [bob](https://github.com/stephenafamo/bob) - SQL query builder and ORM/Factory generator for Go. Successor of SQLBoiler. ⭐ 1616
* [bun](https://github.com/uptrace/bun) - SQL-first Golang ORM. Successor of go-pg. ⭐ 4644
* [cacheme](https://github.com/Yiling-J/cacheme-go) - Schema based, typed Redis caching/memoize framework for Go. ⭐ 24
* [CQL](https://github.com/FrancoLiberali/cql) - Built on top of GORM, adds compile-time verified queries based on auto-generated code. ⭐ 17
* [ent](https://github.com/facebook/ent) - An entity framework for Go. Simple, yet powerful ORM for modeling and querying data. ⭐ 16893
* [go-dbw](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-dbw) - A simple package that encapsulates database operations. ⭐ 16
* [go-firestorm](https://github.com/jschoedt/go-firestorm) - A simple ORM for Google/Firebase Cloud Firestore. ⭐ 53
* [go-sql](https://github.com/rushteam/gosql) - A easy ORM for mysql. ⭐ 178
* [go-sqlbuilder](https://github.com/huandu/go-sqlbuilder) - A flexible and powerful SQL string builder library plus a zero-config ORM. ⭐ 1659
* [go-store](https://github.com/gosuri/go-store) - Simple and fast Redis backed key-value store library for Go. ⭐ 113
* [golobby/orm](https://github.com/golobby/orm) - Simple, fast, type-safe, generic orm for developer happiness. ⭐ 162
* [GORM](https://github.com/go-gorm/gorm) - The fantastic ORM library for Golang, aims to be developer friendly. ⭐ 39456
* [gormt](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gormt) - Mysql database to golang gorm struct. ⭐ 2437
* [gorp](https://github.com/go-gorp/gorp) - Go Relational Persistence, ORM-ish library for Go. ⭐ 3755
* [grimoire](https://github.com/Fs02/grimoire) - Grimoire is a database access layer and validation for golang. (Support: MySQL, PostgreSQL and SQLite3). ⭐ 161
* [lore](https://github.com/abrahambotros/lore) - Simple and lightweight pseudo-ORM/pseudo-struct-mapping environment for Go. ⭐ 14
* [marlow](https://github.com/marlow/marlow) - Generated ORM from project structs for compile time safety assurances. ⭐ 12
* [pop/soda](https://github.com/gobuffalo/pop) - Database migration, creation, ORM, etc... for MySQL, PostgreSQL, and SQLite. ⭐ 1497
* [Prisma](https://github.com/prisma/prisma-client-go) - Prisma Client Go, Typesafe database access for Go. ⭐ 2287
* [reform](https://github.com/go-reform/reform) - Better ORM for Go, based on non-empty interfaces and code generation. ⭐ 1455
* [rel](https://github.com/go-rel/rel) - Modern Database Access Layer for Golang - Testable, Extendable and Crafted Into a Clean and Elegant API. ⭐ 781
* [SQLBoiler](https://github.com/volatiletech/sqlboiler) - ORM generator. Generate a featureful and blazing-fast ORM tailored to your database schema. ⭐ 6973
* [upper.io/db](https://github.com/upper/db) - Single interface for interacting with different data sources through the use of adapters that wrap mature database drivers. ⭐ 3639
* [XORM](https://gitea.com/xorm/xorm) - Simple and powerful ORM for Go. (Support: MySQL, MyMysql, PostgreSQL, Tidb, SQLite3, MsSql and Oracle).
* [Zoom](https://github.com/albrow/zoom) - Blazing-fast datastore and querying engine built on Redis. ⭐ 313

* [modup](https://github.com/chaindead/modup) - Terminal UI for Go dependency updates with outdated module detection and selective upgrading. ⭐ 61
* [syft](https://github.com/anchore/syft) - A CLI tool and Go library for generating a Software Bill of Materials (SBOM) from container images and filesystems. ⭐ 8313

## Query Language

* [api-fu](https://github.com/ccbrown/api-fu) - Comprehensive GraphQL implementation. ⭐ 57
* [dasel](https://github.com/tomwright/dasel) - Query and update data structures using selectors from the command line. Comparable to jq/yq but supports JSON, YAML, TOML and XML with zero runtime dependencies. ⭐ 7811
* [gojsonq](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/gojsonq) - A simple Go package to Query over JSON Data. ⭐ 2230
* [goven](https://github.com/SeldonIO/goven) - A drop-in query language for any database schema. ⭐ 63
* [gqlgen](https://github.com/99designs/gqlgen) - go generate based graphql server library. ⭐ 10652
* [grapher](https://github.com/reaganiwadha/grapher) - A GraphQL field builder utilizing Go generics with extra utilities and features. ⭐ 4
* [graphql](https://github.com/neelance/graphql-go) - GraphQL server with a focus on ease of use. ⭐ 4740
* [graphql-go](https://github.com/graphql-go/graphql) - Implementation of GraphQL for Go. ⭐ 10146
* [gws](https://github.com/Zaba505/gws) - Apollos' "GraphQL over Websocket" client and server implementation. ⭐ 6
* [jsonpath](https://github.com/AsaiYusuke/jsonpath) - A query library for retrieving part of JSON based on JSONPath syntax. ⭐ 30
* [jsonql](https://github.com/elgs/jsonql) - JSON query expression library in Golang. ⭐ 279
* [jsonslice](https://github.com/bhmj/jsonslice) - Jsonpath queries with advanced filters. ⭐ 92
* [mql](https://github.com/hashicorp/mql) - Model Query Language (mql) is a query language for your database models. ⭐ 65
* [play](https://github.com/paololazzari/play) - A TUI playground to experiment with your favorite programs, such as grep, sed, awk, jq and yq. ⭐ 536
* [rql](https://github.com/a8m/rql) - Resource Query Language for REST API. ⭐ 363
* [rqp](https://github.com/timsolov/rest-query-parser) - Query Parser for REST API. Filtering, validations, both AND, OR operations are supported directly in the query. ⭐ 89
* [straf](https://github.com/SonicRoshan/straf) - Easily Convert Golang structs to GraphQL objects. ⭐ 40

## Reflection

* [copy](https://github.com/gotidy/copy) - Package for fast copying structs of different types. ⭐ 52
* [Deepcopier](https://github.com/ulule/deepcopier) - Simple struct copying for Go. ⭐ 461
* [go-deepcopy](https://github.com/tiendc/go-deepcopy) - Fast deep copy library. ⭐ 125
* [goenum](https://github.com/lvyahui8/goenum) - A common enumeration struct based on generics and reflection that allows you to quickly define enumerations and use a set of useful default methods. ⭐ 16
* [gotype](https://github.com/wzshiming/gotype) - Golang source code parsing, usage like reflect package. ⭐ 64
* [gpath](https://github.com/tenntenn/gpath) - Library to simplify access struct fields with Go's expression in reflection. ⭐ 41
* [objwalker](https://github.com/rekby/objwalker) - Walk by go objects with reflection. ⭐ 4
* [reflectpro](https://github.com/gontainer/reflectpro) - Callers, copiers, getters and setters for go. ⭐ 9
* [reflectutils](https://github.com/muir/reflectutils) - Helpers for working with reflection: struct tag parsing; recursive walking; fill value from string. ⭐ 9

## Science and Data Analysis
Libraries for scientific computing and data analyzing.

* [assocentity](https://github.com/ndabAP/assocentity) - Package assocentity returns the average distance from words to a given entity.

* [evaler](https://github.com/soniah/evaler) - Simple floating point arithmetic expression evaluator. ⭐ 50
* [ewma](https://github.com/VividCortex/ewma) - Exponentially-weighted moving averages. ⭐ 451
* [geom](https://github.com/skelterjohn/geom) - 2D geometry for golang. ⭐ 55
* [go-dsp](https://github.com/mjibson/go-dsp) - Digital Signal Processing for Go. ⭐ 904
* [go-estimate](https://github.com/milosgajdos/go-estimate) - State estimation and filtering algorithms in Go. ⭐ 121
* [go-gt](https://github.com/ThePaw/go-gt) - Graph theory algorithms written in "Go" language. ⭐ 11
* [go-hep](https://github.com/go-hep/hep) - A set of libraries and tools for performing High Energy Physics analyses with ease. ⭐ 252
* [godesim](https://github.com/soypat/godesim) - Extended/multivariable ODE solver framework for event-based simulations with simple API. ⭐ 23
* [goent](https://github.com/kzahedi/goent) - GO Implementation of Entropy Measures. ⭐ 36
* [gograph](https://github.com/hmdsefi/gograph) - A golang generic graph library that provides mathematical graph-theory and algorithms. ⭐ 105
* [gonum](https://github.com/gonum/gonum) - Gonum is a set of numeric libraries for the Go programming language. It contains libraries for matrices, statistics, optimization, and more. ⭐ 8288
* [gonum/plot](https://github.com/gonum/plot) - gonum/plot provides an API for building and drawing plots in Go. ⭐ 2939
* [goraph](https://github.com/gyuho/goraph) - Pure Go graph theory library(data structure, algorithm visualization). ⭐ 745
* [gosl](https://github.com/cpmech/gosl) - Go scientific library for linear algebra, FFT, geometry, NURBS, numerical methods, probabilities, optimisation, differential equations, and more. ⭐ 1871
* [GoStats](https://github.com/OGFris/GoStats) - GoStats is an Open Source GoLang library for math statistics mostly used in Machine Learning domains, it covers most of the Statistical measures functions. ⭐ 22
* [graph](https://github.com/yourbasic/graph) - Library of basic graph algorithms. ⭐ 750
* [jsonl-graph](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/jsonl-graph) - Tool to manipulate JSONL graphs with graphviz support. ⭐ 77
* [ode](https://github.com/ChristopherRabotin/ode) - Ordinary differential equation (ODE) solver which supports extended states and channel-based iteration stop conditions. ⭐ 22
* [orb](https://github.com/paulmach/orb) - 2D geometry types with clipping, GeoJSON and Mapbox Vector Tile support. ⭐ 1084
* [pagerank](https://github.com/alixaxel/pagerank) - Weighted PageRank algorithm implemented in Go. ⭐ 87
* [piecewiselinear](https://github.com/sgreben/piecewiselinear) - Tiny linear interpolation library. ⭐ 28
* [PiHex](https://github.com/claygod/PiHex) - Implementation of the "Bailey-Borwein-Plouffe" algorithm for the hexadecimal number Pi. ⭐ 20
* [Poly](https://github.com/bebop/poly) - A Go package for engineering organisms. ⭐ 721
* [rootfinding](https://github.com/khezen/rootfinding) - root-finding algorithms library for finding roots of quadratic functions. ⭐ 12
* [sparse](https://github.com/james-bowman/sparse) - Go Sparse matrix formats for linear algebra supporting scientific and machine learning applications, compatible with gonum matrix libraries. ⭐ 166
* [stats](https://github.com/montanaflynn/stats) - Statistics package with common functions missing from the Golang standard library. ⭐ 3000
* [streamtools](https://github.com/nytlabs/streamtools) - general purpose, graphical tool for dealing with streams of data. ⭐ 1311
* [TextRank](https://github.com/DavidBelicza/TextRank) - TextRank implementation in Golang with extendable features (summarization, weighting, phrase extraction) and multithreading (goroutine) support. ⭐ 222
* [topk](https://github.com/keilerkonzept/topk) - Sliding-window and regular top-K sketches, based on the HeavyKeeper algorithm. ⭐ 16

## Security
Libraries that are used to help make your application more secure.

* [acmetool](https://github.com/hlandau/acme) - ACME (Let's Encrypt) client tool with automatic renewal. ⭐ 2090
* [acopw-go](https://sr.ht/~jamesponddotco/acopw-go/) - Small cryptographically secure password generator package for Go.
* [acra](https://github.com/cossacklabs/acra) - Network encryption proxy to protect database-based applications from data leaks: strong selective encryption, SQL injections prevention, intrusion detection system. ⭐ 1451
* [age](https://github.com/FiloSottile/age) - A simple, modern and secure encryption tool (and Go library) with small explicit keys, no config options, and UNIX-style composability. ⭐ 21144
* [argon2-hashing](https://github.com/andskur/argon2-hashing) - light wrapper around Go's argon2 package that closely mirrors with Go's standard library Bcrypt and simple-scrypt package. ⭐ 25
* [autocert](https://pkg.go.dev/golang.org/x/crypto/acme/autocert) - Auto provision Let's Encrypt certificates and start a TLS server.
* [BadActor](https://github.com/jaredfolkins/badactor) - In-memory, application-driven jailer built in the spirit of fail2ban. ⭐ 324
* [beelzebub](https://github.com/mariocandela/beelzebub) - A secure low code honeypot framework, leveraging AI for System Virtualization. ⭐ 1827
* [booster](https://github.com/anatol/booster) - Fast initramfs generator with full-disk encryption support. ⭐ 619
* [Cameradar](https://github.com/Ullaakut/cameradar) - Tool and library to remotely hack RTSP streams from surveillance cameras. ⭐ 4842
* [certificates](https://github.com/mvmaasakkers/certificates) - An opinionated tool for generating tls certificates. ⭐ 38
* [CertMagic](https://github.com/caddyserver/certmagic) - Mature, robust, and powerful ACME client integration for fully-managed TLS certificate issuance and renewal. ⭐ 5432
* [Coraza](https://github.com/corazawaf/coraza) - Enterprise-ready, modsecurity and OWASP CRS compatible WAF library. ⭐ 3244
* [dongle](https://github.com/golang-module/dongle) - A simple, semantic and developer-friendly golang package for encoding&decoding and encryption&decryption. ⭐ 1098
* [encid](https://github.com/bobg/encid) - Encode and decode encrypted integer IDs. ⭐ 6
* [entpassgen](https://github.com/andreimerlescu/entpassgen) - Entropy Password Generator with extensive command line arguments to generate random strings securely including digits, passwords, and passwords built using obscure dictionary words mixed with symbols and digits. ⭐ 6
* [firewalld-rest](https://github.com/prashantgupta24/firewalld-rest) - A rest application to dynamically update firewalld rules on a linux server. ⭐ 343
* [go-generate-password](https://github.com/m1/go-generate-password) - Password generator that can be used on the cli or as a library. ⭐ 57
* [go-htpasswd](https://github.com/tg123/go-htpasswd) - Apache htpasswd Parser for Go. ⭐ 46
* [go-password-validator](https://github.com/lane-c-wagner/go-password-validator) - Password validator based on raw cryptographic entropy values. ⭐ 565
* [go-peer](https://github.com/number571/go-peer) - A software library for creating secure and anonymous decentralized systems. ⭐ 315
* [go-yara](https://github.com/hillu/go-yara) - Go Bindings for YARA, the "pattern matching swiss knife for malware researchers (and everyone else)". ⭐ 385
* [goArgonPass](https://github.com/dwin/goArgonPass) - Argon2 password hash and verification designed to be compatible with existing Python and PHP implementations. ⭐ 20
* [goSecretBoxPassword](https://github.com/dwin/goSecretBoxPassword) - A probably paranoid package for securely hashing and encrypting passwords. ⭐ 60
* [Interpol](https://github.com/avahidi/interpol) - Rule-based data generator for fuzzing and penetration testing. ⭐ 7
* [lego](https://github.com/go-acme/lego) - Pure Go ACME client library and CLI tool (for use with Let's Encrypt). ⭐ 9227
* [luks.go](https://github.com/anatol/luks.go) - Pure Golang library to manage LUKS partitions. ⭐ 95
* [memguard](https://github.com/awnumar/memguard) - A pure Go library for handling sensitive values in memory. ⭐ 2710
* [multikey](https://github.com/adrianosela/multikey) - An n-out-of-N keys encryption/decryption framework based on Shamir's Secret Sharing algorithm. ⭐ 11
* [nacl](https://github.com/kevinburke/nacl) - Go implementation of the NaCL set of API's. ⭐ 551
* [optimus-go](https://github.com/pjebs/optimus-go) - ID hashing and Obfuscation using Knuth's Algorithm. ⭐ 366
* [passlib](https://github.com/hlandau/passlib) - Futureproof password hashing library. ⭐ 291
* [passwap](https://github.com/zitadel/passwap) - Provides a unified implementation between different password hashing algorithms ⭐ 72
* [qrand](https://github.com/bitfield/qrand) - Client for the ANU Quantum Numbers (AQN) API, providing quantum-mechanically secure random data. ⭐ 17
* [SafeDep/vet](https://github.com/safedep/vet) - Protect against malicious open source packages. ⭐ 939
* [secret](https://github.com/rsjethani/secret) - Prevent your secrets from leaking into logs, std* etc. ⭐ 32
* [secure](https://github.com/unrolled/secure) - HTTP middleware for Go that facilitates some quick security wins. ⭐ 2335
* [secureio](https://github.com/xaionaro-go/secureio) - An keyexchanging+authenticating+encrypting wrapper and multiplexer for io.ReadWriteCloser based on XChaCha20-poly1305, ECDH and ED25519. ⭐ 33
* [simple-scrypt](https://github.com/elithrar/simple-scrypt) - Scrypt package with a simple, obvious API and automatic cost calibration built-in. ⭐ 201
* [ssh-vault](https://github.com/ssh-vault/ssh-vault) - encrypt/decrypt using ssh keys. ⭐ 494
* [sslmgr](https://github.com/adrianosela/sslmgr) - SSL certificates made easy with a high level wrapper around acme/autocert. ⭐ 30
* [teler-waf](https://github.com/kitabisa/teler-waf) - teler-waf is a Go HTTP middleware that provide teler IDS functionality to protect against web-based attacks and improve the security of Go-based web applications. It is highly configurable and easy to integrate into existing Go applications. ⭐ 399
* [themis](https://github.com/cossacklabs/themis) - high-level cryptographic library for solving typical data security tasks (secure data storage, secure messaging, zero-knowledge proof authentication), available for 14 languages, best fit for multi-platform apps. ⭐ 1947
* [urusai](https://github.com/calpa/urusai) - Urusai ("noisy" in Japanese) is a Go implementation of a random HTTP/DNS traffic noise generator that helps protect privacy by creating digital smokescreens while browsing. ⭐ 178

* [bambam](https://github.com/glycerine/bambam) - generator for Cap'n Proto schemas from go. ⭐ 64

* [binstruct](https://github.com/ghostiam/binstruct) - Golang binary decoder for mapping data into the structure. ⭐ 112
* [cbor](https://github.com/fxamacker/cbor) - Small, safe, and easy CBOR encoding and decoding library. ⭐ 1014
* [colfer](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/colfer) - Code generation for the Colfer binary format. ⭐ 756
* [csvutil](https://github.com/jszwec/csvutil) - High Performance, idiomatic CSV record encoding and decoding to native Go structures. ⭐ 1030
* [elastic](https://github.com/epiclabs-io/elastic) - Convert slices, maps or any other unknown value across different types at run-time, no matter what. ⭐ 25
* [fixedwidth](https://github.com/huydang284/fixedwidth) - Fixed-width text formatting (UTF-8 supported). ⭐ 9
* [fwencoder](https://github.com/o1egl/fwencoder) - Fixed width file parser (encoding and decoding library) for Go. ⭐ 27
* [go-capnproto](https://github.com/glycerine/go-capnproto) - Cap'n Proto library and parser for go. ⭐ 287
* [go-codec](https://github.com/ugorji/go) - High Performance, feature-Rich, idiomatic encode, decode and rpc library for msgpack, cbor and json, with runtime-based OR code-generation support. ⭐ 1934
* [go-csvlib](https://github.com/tiendc/go-csvlib) - High level and rich functionalities CSV serialization/deserialization library. ⭐ 19
* [goprotobuf](https://github.com/golang/protobuf) - Go support, in the form of a library and protocol compiler plugin, for Google's protocol buffers. ⭐ 10061
* [gotiny](https://github.com/raszia/gotiny) - Efficient Go serialization library, gotiny is almost as fast as serialization libraries that generate code. ⭐ 21
* [jsoniter](https://github.com/json-iterator/go) - High-performance 100% compatible drop-in replacement of "encoding/json". ⭐ 13939
* [php_session_decoder](https://github.com/yvasiyarov/php_session_decoder) - GoLang library for working with PHP session format and PHP Serialize/Unserialize functions. ⭐ 169
* [pletter](https://github.com/vimeda/pletter) - A standard way to wrap a proto message for message brokers. ⭐ 19
* [structomap](https://github.com/tuvistavie/structomap) - Library to easily and dynamically generate maps from static structures. ⭐ 144
* [unitpacking](https://github.com/recolude/unitpacking) - Library to pack unit vectors into as fewest bytes as possible. ⭐ 7

## Template Engines
Libraries and tools for templating and lexing.

* [ego](https://github.com/benbjohnson/ego) - Lightweight templating language that lets you write templates in Go. Templates are translated into Go and compiled. ⭐ 590
* [extemplate](https://git.sr.ht/~dvko/extemplate) - Tiny wrapper around html/template to allow for easy file-based template inheritance.
* [fasttemplate](https://github.com/valyala/fasttemplate) - Simple and fast template engine. Substitutes template placeholders up to 10x faster than text/template. ⭐ 901
* [gomponents](https://www.gomponents.com) - HTML 5 components in pure Go, that look something like this: func(name string) g.Node { return Div(Class("headline"), g.Textf("Hi %v!", name)) }.
* [got](https://github.com/goradd/got) - A Go code generator inspired by Hero and Fasttemplate. Has include files, custom tag definitions, injected Go code, language translation, and more. ⭐ 38
* [goview](https://github.com/foolin/goview) - Goview is a lightweight, minimalist and idiomatic template library based on golang html/template for building Go web application. ⭐ 466
* [htmgo](https://htmgo.dev) - build simple and scalable systems with go + htmx
* [jet](https://github.com/CloudyKit/jet) - Jet template engine. ⭐ 1380
* [liquid](https://github.com/osteele/liquid) - Go implementation of Shopify Liquid templates. ⭐ 339
* [maroto](https://github.com/johnfercher/maroto) - A maroto way to create PDFs. Maroto is inspired in Bootstrap and uses gofpdf. Fast and simple. ⭐ 2631
* [pongo2](https://github.com/flosch/pongo2) - Django-like template-engine for Go. ⭐ 3024
* [quicktemplate](https://github.com/valyala/quicktemplate) - Fast, powerful, yet easy to use template engine. Converts templates into Go code and then compiles it. ⭐ 3296
* [Razor](https://github.com/sipin/gorazor) - Razor view engine for Golang. ⭐ 882
* [Soy](https://github.com/robfig/soy) - Closure templates (aka Soy templates) for Go, following the official spec. ⭐ 177
* [sprout](https://github.com/go-sprout/sprout) - Useful template functions for Go templates. ⭐ 208
* [tbd](https://github.com/lucasepe/tbd) - A really simple way to create text templates with placeholders - exposes extra builtin Git repo metadata. ⭐ 27
* [templ](https://github.com/a-h/templ) - A HTML templating language that has great developer tooling. ⭐ 10034
* [templator](https://github.com/alesr/templator) - A type-safe HTML template rendering engine for Go. ⭐ 7

## Testing
Libraries for testing codebases and generating test data.
### Testing Frameworks

* [apitest](https://apitest.dev) - Simple and extensible behavioural testing library for REST based services or HTTP handlers that supports mocking external http calls and rendering of sequence diagrams.
* [arch-go](https://github.com/arch-go/arch-go) - Architecture testing tool for Go projects. (245)
* [assert](https://github.com/go-playground/assert) - Basic Assertion Library used along side native go testing, with building blocks for custom assertions. (68)
* [baloo](https://github.com/h2non/baloo) - Expressive and versatile end-to-end HTTP API testing made easy. (782)
* [be](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/be) - The minimalist generic test assertion library. (131)
* [biff](https://github.com/fulldump/biff) - Bifurcation testing framework, BDD compatible. (14)
* [charlatan](https://github.com/percolate/charlatan) - Tool to generate fake interface implementations for tests. (204)
* [commander](https://github.com/SimonBaeumer/commander) - Tool for testing cli applications on windows, linux and osx. (229)
* [cupaloy](https://github.com/bradleyjkemp/cupaloy) - Simple snapshot testing addon for your test framework. (328)
* [dbcleaner](https://github.com/khaiql/dbcleaner) - Clean database for testing purpose, inspired by database_cleaner in Ruby. (163)
* [dft](https://github.com/abecodes/dft) - Lightweight, zero dependency docker containers for testing (or more). (19)
* [dsunit](https://github.com/viant/dsunit) - Datastore testing for SQL, NoSQL, structured files. (45)
* [embedded-postgres](https://github.com/fergusstrange/embedded-postgres) - Run a real Postgres database locally on Linux, OSX or Windows as part of another Go application or test. (1116)
* [endly](https://github.com/viant/endly) - Declarative end to end functional testing. (267)
* [envite](https://github.com/PerimeterX/envite) - Dev and testing environment management framework. (4)

* [gomega](https://onsi.github.io/gomega/) - Rspec like matcher/assertion library.
* [Gont](https://github.com/stv0g/gont) - Go network testing toolkit for testing building complex network topologies using Linux namespaces.
* [gospecify](https://github.com/stesla/gospecify) - This provides a BDD syntax for testing your Go code. It should be familiar to anybody who has used libraries such as rspec. (52)
* [gosuite](https://github.com/pavlo/gosuite) - Brings lightweight test suites with setup/teardown facilities to testing by leveraging Go1.7's Subtests. (12)

* [Hamcrest](https://github.com/rdrdr/hamcrest) - fluent framework for declarative Matcher objects that, when applied to input values, produce self-describing results. (30)
* [httpexpect](https://github.com/gavv/httpexpect) - Concise, declarative, and easy to use end-to-end HTTP and REST API testing. (2710)

* [testcase](https://github.com/adamluzsi/testcase) - Idiomatic testing framework for Behavior Driven Development. (127)
* [testcerts](https://github.com/madflojo/testcerts) - Dynamically generate self-signed certificates and certificate authorities within your test functions. (84)
* [testcontainers-go](https://github.com/testcontainers/testcontainers-go) - A Go package that makes it simple to create and clean up container-based dependencies for automated integration/smoke tests. The clean, easy-to-use API enables developers to programmatically define containers that should be run as part of a test and clean up those resources when the test is done. (4637)
* [testfixtures](https://github.com/go-testfixtures/testfixtures) - A helper for Rails' like test fixtures to test database applications. (1216)

* [wstest](https://github.com/posener/wstest) - Websocket client for unit-testing a websocket http.Handler. (102)
### Mock

* [connexions](https://github.com/cubahno/connexions) - Combine multiple APIs with meaningful responses, configurable latency and error codes based on OpenAPI 3.0 specifications and files. (3)

* [govcr](https://github.com/seborama/govcr) - HTTP mock for Golang: record and replay HTTP interactions for offline testing. (196)
* [hoverfly](https://github.com/SpectoLabs/hoverfly) - HTTP(S) proxy for recording and simulating REST/SOAP APIs with extensible middleware and easy-to-use CLI. (2461)

* [minimock](https://github.com/gojuno/minimock) - Mock generator for Go interfaces. (744)
* [mockery](https://github.com/vektra/mockery) - Tool to generate Go interfaces. (6977)
* [mockfs](https://github.com/balinomad/go-mockfs) - Mock filesystem for Go testing with error injection and latency simulation, built on testing/fstest.MapFS. (7)
* [mockhttp](https://github.com/tv42/mockhttp) - Mock object for Go http.ResponseWriter. (23)
* [mooncake](https://github.com/GuilhermeCaruso/mooncake) - A simple way to generate mocks for multiple purposes. (18)
* [moq](https://github.com/matryer/moq) - Utility that generates a struct from any interface. The struct can be used in test code as a mock of the interface. (2172)
* [moxie](https://lesiw.io/moxie) - Generate mock methods on embedded structs.
* [pgxmock](https://github.com/pashagolub/pgxmock) - A mock library implementing pgx - PostgreSQL Driver and Toolkit. (559)
* [timex](https://github.com/cabify/timex) - A test-friendly replacement for the native time package. (71)
* [xgo](https://github.com/xhd2015/xgo) - A general pureposed function mocking library. (429)
