## Text Processing
See also Natural Language Processing and Text Analysis.
### Formatters

* [address](https://github.com/bojanz/address) - Handles address representation, validation and formatting. (82)
* [align](https://github.com/Guitarbum722/align) - A general purpose application that aligns text. (84)
* [bytes](https://github.com/labstack/gommon/tree/master/bytes) - Formats and parses numeric byte values (10K, 2M, 3G, etc.).
* [go-fixedwidth](https://github.com/ianlopshire/go-fixedwidth) - Fixed-width text formatting (encoder/decoder with reflection). (87)
* [go-humanize](https://github.com/dustin/go-humanize) - Formatters for time, numbers, and memory size to human readable format. (4791)
* [gotabulate](https://github.com/bndr/gotabulate) - Easily pretty-print your tabular data with Go. (339)
* [sq](https://github.com/neilotoole/sq) - Convert data from SQL databases or document formats like CSV or Excel into formats such as JSON, Excel, CSV, HTML, Markdown, XML, and YAML. (2426)
* [textwrap](https://github.com/isbm/textwrap) - Wraps text at end of lines. Implementation of textwrap module from Python. (6)
### Markup Languages

* [bafi](https://github.com/mmalcek/bafi) - Universal JSON, BSON, YAML, XML translator to ANY format using templates. (112)
* [bbConvert](https://github.com/CalebQ42/bbConvert) - Converts bbCode to HTML that allows you to add support for custom bbCode tags. (12)
* [blackfriday](https://github.com/russross/blackfriday) - Markdown processor in Go. (5616)
* [go-output-format](https://github.com/drewstinnett/go-output-format) - Output go structures into multiple formats (YAML/JSON/etc) in your command line app. (18)
* [go-toml](https://github.com/pelletier/go-toml) - Go library for the TOML format with query support and handy cli tools. (1902)
* [goldmark](https://github.com/yuin/goldmark) - A Markdown parser written in Go. Easy to extend, standard (CommonMark) compliant, well structured. (4576)
* [goq](https://github.com/andrewstuart/goq) - Declarative unmarshalling of HTML using struct tags with jQuery syntax (uses GoQuery). (271)
* [html-to-markdown](https://github.com/JohannesKaufmann/html-to-markdown) - Convert HTML to Markdown. Even works with entire websites and can be extended through rules. (3374)
* [htmlquery](https://github.com/antchfx/htmlquery) - An XPath query package for HTML, lets you extract data or evaluate from HTML documents by an XPath expression. (780)
* [htmlyaml](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/htmlyaml) - Rich rendering of YAML as HTML in Go. (5)
* [htree](https://github.com/bobg/htree) - Traverse, navigate, filter, and otherwise process trees of html.Node objects. (4)
* [mxj](https://github.com/clbanning/mxj) - Encode / decode XML as JSON or map[string]interface{}; extract values with dot-notation paths and wildcards. Replaces x2j and j2x packages. (633)
* [toml](https://github.com/BurntSushi/toml) - TOML configuration format (encoder/decoder with reflection). (4891)
### Parsers/Encoders/Decoders

* [allot](https://github.com/sbstjn/allot) - Placeholder and wildcard text parsing for CLI tools and bots. (60)
* [codetree](https://github.com/aerogo/codetree) - Parses indented code (python, pixy, scarlet, etc.) and returns a tree structure. (25)
* [commonregex](https://github.com/mingrammer/commonregex) - A collection of common regular expressions for Go. (900)
* [did](https://github.com/ockam-network/did) - DID (Decentralized Identifiers) Parser and Stringer in Go. (95)
* [doi](https://github.com/hscells/doi) - Document object identifier (doi) parser in Go. (11)
* [editorconfig-core-go](https://github.com/editorconfig/editorconfig-core-go) - Editorconfig file parser and manipulator for Go. (150)
* [encdec](https://github.com/mickep76/encdec) - Package provides a generic interface to encoders and decoders.
* [go-fasttld](https://github.com/elliotwutingfeng/go-fasttld) - High performance effective top level domains (eTLD) extraction module. (38)
* [go-nmea](https://github.com/adrianmo/go-nmea) - NMEA parser library for the Go language. (255)
* [go-querystring](https://github.com/google/go-querystring) - Go library for encoding structs into URL query parameters. (2129)
* [go-vcard](https://github.com/emersion/go-vcard) - Parse and format vCard. (123)
* [godump](https://github.com/yassinebenaid/godump) - Pretty print any GO variable with ease, an alternative to Go's fmt.Printf("%#v"). (223)
* [godump (goforj)](https://github.com/goforj/godump) - Pretty-print Go structs with Laravel/Symfony-style dumps, full type info, colorized CLI output, cycle detection, and private field access. (1680)
* [gofeed](https://github.com/mmcdole/gofeed) - Parse RSS and Atom feeds in Go. (2804)
* [gographviz](https://github.com/awalterschulze/gographviz) - Parses the Graphviz DOT language. (568)
* [gonameparts](https://github.com/polera/gonameparts) - Parses human names into individual name parts. (43)
* [ltsv](https://github.com/Wing924/ltsv) - High performance LTSV (Labeled Tab Separated Value) reader for Go. (10)
* [normalize](https://github.com/avito-tech/normalize) - Sanitize, normalize and compare fuzzy text. (54)
* [parseargs-go](https://github.com/nproc/parseargs-go) - string argument parser that understands quotes and backslashes. (10)
* [prattle](https://github.com/askeladdk/prattle) - Scan and parse LL(1) grammars simply and efficiently. (8)
* [sh](https://github.com/mvdan/sh) - Shell parser and formatter. (8430)
* [tokenizer](https://github.com/bzick/tokenizer) - Parse any string, slice or infinite buffer to any tokens. (138)
* [vdf](https://github.com/andygrunwald/vdf) - A Lexer and Parser for Valves Data Format (known as vdf) written in Go. (62)
* [when](https://github.com/olebedev/when) - Natural EN and RU language date/time parser with pluggable rules. (1458)
* [xj2go](https://github.com/stackerzzq/xj2go) - Convert xml or json to go struct. (36)
### Regular Expressions

* [genex](https://github.com/alixaxel/genex) - Count and expand Regular Expressions into all matching Strings. (76)
* [go-wildcard](https://github.com/IGLOU-EU/go-wildcard) - Simple and lightweight wildcard pattern matching. (99)
* [goregen](https://github.com/zach-klippenstein/goregen) - Library for generating random strings from regular expressions. (92)
* [regroup](https://github.com/oriser/regroup) - Match regex expression named groups into go struct using struct tags and automatic parsing. (150)
* [rex](https://github.com/hedhyw/rex) - Regular expressions builder. (210)
### Sanitation

* [bluemonday](https://github.com/microcosm-cc/bluemonday) - HTML Sanitizer. (3616)
* [gofuckyourself](https://github.com/JoshuaDoes/gofuckyourself) - A sanitization-based swear filter for Go. (68)
### Scrapers

* [colly](https://github.com/asciimoo/colly) - Fast and Elegant Scraping Framework for Gophers. (25049)
* [dataflowkit](https://github.com/slotix/dataflowkit) - Web scraping Framework to turn websites into structured data. (710)
* [go-recipe](https://github.com/kkyr/go-recipe) - A package for scraping recipes from websites. (32)
* [go-sitemap-parser](https://github.com/aafeher/go-sitemap-parser) - Go language library for parsing Sitemaps. (5)
* [GoQuery](https://github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery) - GoQuery brings a syntax and a set of features similar to jQuery to the Go language. (14913)
* [pagser](https://github.com/foolin/pagser) - Pagser is a simple, extensible, configurable parse and deserialize html page to struct based on goquery and struct tags for golang crawler. (111)
* [Tagify](https://github.com/zoomio/tagify) - Produces a set of tags from given source. (39)
* [walker](https://github.com/cyucelen/walker) - Seamlessly fetch paginated data from any source. Simple and high performance API scraping included. (14)
* [xurls](https://github.com/mvdan/xurls) - Extract urls from text. (1246)
### RSS

* [podcast](https://github.com/eduncan911/podcast) - iTunes Compliant and RSS 2.0 Podcast Generator in Golang (138)
### Utility/Miscellaneous

* [go-runewidth](https://github.com/mattn/go-runewidth) - Functions to get fixed width of the character or string. (674)
* [kace](https://github.com/codemodus/kace) - Common case conversions covering common initialisms. (21)
* [lancet](https://github.com/duke-git/lancet) - A comprehensive, Lodash-like utility library for Go (5271)
* [petrovich](https://github.com/striker2000/petrovich) - Petrovich is the library which inflects Russian names to given grammatical case. (51)
* [radix](https://github.com/yourbasic/radix) - Fast string sorting algorithm. (196)
* [TySug](https://github.com/Dynom/TySug) - Alternative suggestions with respect to keyboard layouts. (19)
* [w2vgrep](https://github.com/arunsupe/semantic-grep) - A semantic grep tool using word embeddings to find semantically similar matches. For example, searching for "death" will find "dead", "killing", "murder". (1203)

## UUID
Libraries for working with UUIDs.

* [fastuuid](https://github.com/rekby/fastuuid) - Fast generate UUIDv4 as string or bytes. ⭐ 1
* [goid](https://github.com/jakehl/goid) - Generate and Parse RFC4122 compliant V4 UUIDs. ⭐ 41
* [gouid](https://github.com/twharmon/gouid) - Generate cryptographically secure random string IDs with just one allocation. ⭐ 26
* [guid](https://github.com/sdrapkin/guid) - Fast cryptographically safe Guid generator for Go (~10x faster than uuid). ⭐ 73
* [nanoid](https://github.com/aidarkhanov/nanoid) - A tiny and efficient Go unique string ID generator. ⭐ 62
* [sno](https://github.com/muyo/sno) - Compact, sortable and fast unique IDs with embedded metadata. ⭐ 94
* [ulid](https://github.com/oklog/ulid) - Go implementation of ULID (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier). ⭐ 4981
* [uniq](https://gitlab.com/skilstak/code/go/uniq) - No hassle safe, fast unique identifiers with commands. ⭐ 3
* [uuid](https://github.com/agext/uuid) - Generate, encode, and decode UUIDs v1 with fast or cryptographic-quality random node identifier. ⭐ 18
* [uuid](https://github.com/gofrs/uuid) - Implementation of Universally Unique Identifier (UUID). Supports both creation and parsing of UUIDs. Actively maintained fork of satori uuid. ⭐ 1761
* [uuid](https://github.com/google/uuid) - Go package for UUIDs based on RFC 4122 and DCE 1.1: Authentication and Security Services. ⭐ 5983
* [uuidcheck](https://github.com/ashwingopalsamy/uuidcheck) - A tiny, dependency-free Go library that validates UUIDs against standard RFC 4122 formatting, converts UUIDv7() into UTC timestamps. ⭐ 5
* [wuid](https://github.com/edwingeng/wuid) - An extremely fast globally unique number generator. ⭐ 545
* [xid](https://github.com/rs/xid) - Xid is a globally unique id generator library, ready to be safely used directly in your server code. ⭐ 4248

### Middlewares

* [client-timing](https://github.com/posener/client-timing) - An HTTP client for Server-Timing header. (25)

* [go-fault](https://github.com/github/go-fault) - Fault injection middleware for Go. (511)
* [Limiter](https://github.com/ulule/limiter) - Dead simple rate limit middleware for Go. (2323)
* [ln-paywall](https://github.com/philippgille/ln-paywall) - Go middleware for monetizing APIs on a per-request basis with the Lightning Network (Bitcoin). (155)
* [mid](https://github.com/bobg/mid) - Miscellaneous HTTP middleware features: idiomatic error return from handlers; receive/respond with JSON data; request tracing; and more. (10)
* [rk-gin](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-gin) - Middleware for Gin framework with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc. (51)
* [rk-grpc](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-grpc) - Middleware for gRPC with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc. (81)

* [XFF](https://github.com/sebest/xff) - Handle X-Forwarded-For header and friends. (100)
* [alice](https://github.com/justinas/alice) - Painless middleware chaining for Go. (3353)
* [catena](https://github.com/codemodus/catena) - http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain"). (9)
* [chain](https://github.com/codemodus/chain) - Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware"). (61)
* [gores](https://github.com/alioygur/gores) - Go package that handles HTML, JSON, XML and etc. responses. Useful for RESTful APIs. (106)

* [httprouter](https://github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter) - High performance router. Use this and the standard http handlers to form a very high performance web framework. (17108)
* [httptreemux](https://github.com/dimfeld/httptreemux) - High-speed, flexible tree-based HTTP router for Go. Inspiration from httprouter. (621)
* [lars](https://github.com/go-playground/lars) - Is a lightweight, fast and extensible zero allocation HTTP router for Go used to create customizable frameworks. (384)
* [mux](https://github.com/gorilla/mux) - Powerful URL router and dispatcher for golang. (21786)
* [nchi](https://github.com/muir/nchi) - chi-like router built on httprouter with dependency injection based middleware wrappers (18)

* [ozzo-routing](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing) - An extremely fast Go (golang) HTTP router that supports regular expression route matching. Comes with full support for building RESTful APIs. (455)
* [pure](https://github.com/go-playground/pure) - Is a lightweight HTTP router that sticks to the std "net/http" implementation. (154)

* [gosddl](https://github.com/MonaxGT/gosddl) - Converter from SDDL-string to user-friendly JSON. SDDL consist of four part: Owner, Primary Group, DACL, SACL. ⭐ 11

## Zero Trust
Libraries and tools to implement Zero Trust architectures.

* [Cosign](https://github.com/sigstore/cosign) - Container Signing, Verification and Storage in an OCI registry. ⭐ 5622
* [in-toto](https://github.com/in-toto/in-toto-golang) - Go implementation of the in-toto (provides a framework to protect the integrity of the software supply chain) python reference implementation. ⭐ 144
* [OpenZiti](https://github.com/openziti/ziti) - A full, open source zero trust overlay network. Including numerous SDKs for numerous languages such as golang allowing you to embed zero trust principles directly into your applications. The OpenZiti Test Kitchen has numerous examples to draw inspiration from including a zero trust ssh client - zssh ⭐ 3848
* [Spiffe-Vault](https://github.com/philips-labs/spiffe-vault) - Utilizes Spiffe JWT authentication with Hashicorp Vault for secretless authentication. ⭐ 97
* [Spire](https://github.com/spiffe/spire) - SPIRE (the SPIFFE Runtime Environment) is a toolchain of APIs for establishing trust between software systems across a wide variety of hosting platforms. ⭐ 2198

## Code Analysis
Source code analysis tools, also known as Static Application Security Testing (SAST) Tools.

* [apicompat](https://github.com/bradleyfalzon/apicompat) - Checks recent changes to a Go project for backwards incompatible changes. ⭐ 181
* [asty](https://github.com/asty-org/asty) - Converts golang AST to JSON and JSON to AST. ⭐ 87
* [blanket](https://gitlab.com/verygoodsoftwarenotvirus/blanket) - blanket is a tool that helps you catch functions which don't have direct unit tests in your Go packages. ⭐ 2
* [ChainJacking](https://github.com/Checkmarx/chainjacking) - Find which of your Go lang direct GitHub dependencies is susceptible to ChainJacking attack. ⭐ 61
* [Chronos](https://github.com/amit-davidson/Chronos) - Detects race conditions statically ⭐ 438
* [dupl](https://github.com/mibk/dupl) - Tool for code clone detection. ⭐ 362
* [errcheck](https://github.com/kisielk/errcheck) - Errcheck is a program for checking for unchecked errors in Go programs. ⭐ 2472
* [fatcontext](https://github.com/Crocmagnon/fatcontext) - Fatcontext detects nested contexts in loops or function literals. ⭐ 65
* [go-checkstyle](https://github.com/qiniu/checkstyle) - checkstyle is a style check tool like java checkstyle. This tool inspired by java checkstyle, golint. The style referred to some points in Go Code Review Comments. ⭐ 130
* [go-cleanarch](https://github.com/roblaszczak/go-cleanarch) - go-cleanarch was created to validate Clean Architecture rules, like a The Dependency Rule and interaction between packages in your Go projects. ⭐ 963
* [go-critic](https://github.com/go-critic/go-critic) - source code linter that brings checks that are currently not implemented in other linters. ⭐ 2028
* [go-mod-outdated](https://github.com/psampaz/go-mod-outdated) - An easy way to find outdated dependencies of your Go projects. ⭐ 664
* [goast-viewer](https://github.com/yuroyoro/goast-viewer) - Web based Golang AST visualizer. ⭐ 790
* [goimports](https://pkg.go.dev/golang.org/x/tools/cmd/goimports) - Tool to fix (add, remove) your Go imports automatically.
* [golang-ifood-sdk](https://github.com/arxdsilva/golang-ifood-sdk) - iFood API SDK. ⭐ 13
* [golangci-lint](https://github.com/golangci/golangci-lint) -  ⭐ 18421
* [golines](https://github.com/segmentio/golines) - Formatter that automatically shortens long lines in Go code. ⭐ 1134
* [GoPlantUML](https://github.com/jfeliu007/goplantuml) - Library and CLI that generates text plantump class diagram containing information about structures and interfaces with the relationship among them. ⭐ 2078
* [goreturns](https://github.com/sqs/goreturns) - Adds zero-value return statements to match the func return types. ⭐ 536
* [gostatus](https://github.com/shurcooL/gostatus) - Command line tool, shows the status of repositories that contain Go packages. ⭐ 245
* [lint](https://github.com/surullabs/lint) - Run linters as part of go test. ⭐ 66

* [terraform-provider-openapi](https://github.com/dikhan/terraform-provider-openapi) - Terraform provider plugin that dynamically configures itself at runtime based on an OpenAPI document (formerly known as swagger file) containing the definitions of the APIs exposed. (279)
* [tf-profile](https://github.com/datarootsio/tf-profile) - Profiler for Terraform runs. Generate global stats, resource-level stats or visualizations. (163)
* [tlm](https://github.com/yusufcanb/tlm) - Local cli copilot, powered by CodeLLaMa (1466)
* [traefik](https://github.com/containous/traefik) - Reverse proxy and load balancer with support for multiple backends. (61403)
* [trubka](https://github.com/xitonix/trubka) - A CLI tool to manage and troubleshoot Apache Kafka clusters with the ability of generically publishing/consuming protocol buffer and plain text events to/from Kafka. (337)
* [uTask](https://github.com/ovh/utask) - Automation engine that models and executes business processes declared in yaml. (1352)
* [Vegeta](https://github.com/tsenart/vegeta) - HTTP load testing tool and library. It's over 9000! (24886)
* [wait-for](https://github.com/dnnrly/wait-for) - Wait for something to happen (from the command line) before continuing. Easy orchestration of Docker services and other things. (17)
* [Wide](https://wide.b3log.org/login) - Web-based IDE for Teams using Golang.
* [winrm-cli](https://github.com/masterzen/winrm-cli) - Cli tool to remotely execute commands on Windows machines. (172)
### Other Software
Where to discover new Go libraries.

* [Better Go Playground](https://goplay.tools) - Go playground with syntax highlight, code completion and other features.
* [blocky](https://github.com/0xERR0R/blocky) - Fast and lightweight DNS proxy as ad-blocker for local network with many features. (6056)
* [bluetuith](https://github.com/bluetuith-org/bluetuith) - TUI Bluetooth manager for Linux. (1292)
* [borg](https://github.com/crufter/borg) - Terminal based search engine for bash snippets. (1609)
* [boxed](https://github.com/tejo/boxed) - Dropbox based blog engine. (78)
* [Chapar](https://github.com/chapar-rest/chapar) - Chapar is a a cross-platform Postman alternative built with go, aims to help developers to test their api endpoints. it support http and grpc protocols. (688)
* [Cherry](https://github.com/rafael-santiago/cherry) - Tiny webchat server in Go. (298)
* [Circuit](https://github.com/gocircuit/circuit) - Circuit is a programmable platform-as-a-service (PaaS) and/or Infrastructure-as-a-Service (IaaS), for management, discovery, synchronization and orchestration of services and hosts comprising cloud applications. (1982)
* [Comcast](https://github.com/tylertreat/Comcast) - Simulate bad network connections. (10495)
* [confd](https://github.com/kelseyhightower/confd) - Manage local application configuration files using templates and data from etcd or consul. (8429)
* [crawley](https://github.com/s0rg/crawley) - Web scraper/crawler for cli. (328)
* [croc](https://github.com/schollz/croc) - Easily and securely send files or folders from one computer to another. (34051)
* [Documize](https://github.com/documize/community) - Modern wiki software that integrates data from SaaS tools. (2361)
* [dp](https://github.com/scryinfo/dp) - Through SDK for data exchange with blockchain, developers can get easy access to DAPP development. (78)
* [drive](https://github.com/odeke-em/drive) - Google Drive client for the commandline. (6747)
* [Duplicacy](https://github.com/gilbertchen/duplicacy) - A cross-platform network and cloud backup tool based on the idea of lock-free deduplication. (5613)
* [fjira](https://github.com/mk-5/fjira) - A fuzzy-search based terminal UI application for Attlasian Jira (252)
* [Gebug](https://github.com/moshebe/gebug) - A tool that makes debugging of Dockerized Go applications super easy by enabling Debugger and Hot-Reload features, seamlessly. (634)
* [gfile](https://github.com/Antonito/gfile) - Securely transfer files between two computers, without any third party, over WebRTC. (757)
* [Go Package Store](https://github.com/shurcooL/Go-Package-Store) - App that displays updates for the Go packages in your GOPATH. (897)
* [go-peerflix](https://github.com/Sioro-Neoku/go-peerflix) - Video streaming torrent client. (475)
* [goblin](https://goblin.run) - Cloud builder for CLI's written in go lang
* [GoBoy](https://github.com/Humpheh/goboy) - Nintendo Game Boy Color emulator written in Go. (2636)
* [gocc](https://github.com/goccmack/gocc) - Gocc is a compiler kit for Go written in Go. (655)
* [GoDocTooltip](https://github.com/diankong/GoDocTooltip) - Chrome extension for Go Doc sites, which shows function description as tooltip at function list. (13)
* [Gokapi](https://github.com/Forceu/gokapi) - Lightweight server to share files, which expire after a set amount of downloads or days. Similar to Firefox Send, but without public upload. (2579)
* [GoLand](https://jetbrains.com/go) - Full featured cross-platform Go IDE.
* [GoNB](https://github.com/janpfeifer/gonb) - Interactive Go programming with Jupyter Notebooks (also works in VSCode, Binder and Google's Colab). (977)
* [Gor](https://github.com/buger/gor) - Http traffic replication tool, for replaying traffic from production to stage/dev environments in real-time. (19236)
* [Guora](https://github.com/meloalright/guora) - A self-hosted Quora like web application written in Go. (677)
* [hoofli](https://github.com/dnnrly/hoofli) - Generate PlantUML diagrams from Chrome or Firefox network inspections. (11)
* [hotswap](https://github.com/edwingeng/hotswap) - A complete solution to reload your go code without restarting your server, interrupting or blocking any ongoing procedure. (418)
* [hugo](https://gohugo.io/) - Fast and Modern Static Website Engine.
* [ide](https://github.com/thestrukture/ide) - Browser accessible IDE. Designed for Go with Go. (363)
* [joincap](https://github.com/assafmo/joincap) - Command-line utility for merging multiple pcap files together. (220)
* [JuiceFS](https://github.com/juicedata/juicefs) - Distributed POSIX file system built on top of Redis and AWS S3. (13156)
* [Juju](https://jujucharms.com/) - Cloud-agnostic service deployment and orchestration - supports EC2, Azure, Openstack, MAAS and more.
* [Layli](https://layli.app) - Draw pretty layout diagrams as code.
* [Leaps](https://github.com/jeffail/leaps) - Pair programming service using Operational Transforms. (756)
* [lgo](https://github.com/yunabe/lgo) - Interactive Go programming with Jupyter. It supports code completion, code inspection and 100% Go compatibility. (2458)
* [limetext](https://limetext.github.io) - Lime Text is a powerful and elegant text editor primarily developed in Go that aims to be a Free and open-source software successor to Sublime Text.
* [LiteIDE](https://github.com/visualfc/liteide) - LiteIDE is a simple, open source, cross-platform Go IDE. (7757)
* [mockingjay](https://github.com/quii/mockingjay-server) - Fake HTTP servers and consumer driven contracts from one configuration file. You can also make the server randomly misbehave to help do more realistic performance tests. (568)
* [myLG](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/mylg) - Command Line Network Diagnostic tool written in Go. (2718)
* [naclpipe](https://github.com/unix4fun/naclpipe) - Simple NaCL EC25519 based crypto pipe tool written in Go. (23)
* [Neo-cowsay](https://github.com/Code-Hex/Neo-cowsay) - 🐮 cowsay is reborn. for a New Era. (341)
* [nes](https://github.com/fogleman/nes) - Nintendo Entertainment System (NES) emulator written in Go. (5638)
* [Orbit](https://github.com/gulien/orbit) - A simple tool for running commands and generating files from templates. (188)
* [peg](https://github.com/pointlander/peg) - Peg, Parsing Expression Grammar, is an implementation of a Packrat parser generator. (1099)
* [Plik](https://github.com/root-gg/plik) - Plik is a temporary file upload system (Wetransfer like) in Go. (1691)
* [portal](https://github.com/SpatiumPortae/portal) - Portal is a quick and easy command-line file transfer utility from any computer to another. (1737)
* [restic](https://github.com/restic/restic) - De-duplicating backup program. (32045)
* [sake](https://github.com/alajmo/sake) - sake is a command runner for local and remote hosts. (743)
* [scc](https://github.com/boyter/scc) - Sloc Cloc and Code, a very fast accurate code counter with complexity calculations and COCOMO estimates. (8006)
* [Seaweed File System](https://github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs) - Fast, Simple and Scalable Distributed File System with O(1) disk seek. (10)
* [shell2http](https://github.com/msoap/shell2http) - Executing shell commands via http server (for prototyping or remote control). (1469)
* [Snitch](https://github.com/lucasgomide/snitch) - Simple way to notify your team and many tools when someone has deployed any application via Tsuru. (16)
* [sonic](https://github.com/go-sonic/sonic) - Sonic is a Go Blogging Platform. Simple and Powerful. (2118)
* [Stack Up](https://github.com/pressly/sup) - Stack Up, a super simple deployment tool - just Unix - think of it like 'make' for a network of servers. (2514)
* [stew](https://github.com/marwanhawari/stew) - An independent package manager for compiled binaries. (325)
* [syncthing](https://syncthing.net/) - Open, decentralized file synchronization tool and protocol.
* [tcpdog](https://github.com/mehrdadrad/tcpdog) - eBPF based TCP observability. (261)
* [tinycare-tui](https://github.com/DMcP89/tinycare-tui) - Small terminal app that shows git commits from the last 24 hours and week, current weather, some self care advice, a joke, and you current todo list tasks. (16)
* [toxiproxy](https://github.com/shopify/toxiproxy) - Proxy to simulate network and system conditions for automated tests. (11809)
* [tsuru](https://tsuru.io/) - Extensible and open source Platform as a Service software.
* [vaku](https://github.com/lingrino/vaku) - CLI & API for folder-based functions in Vault like copy, move, and search. (158)
* [vFlow](https://github.com/VerizonDigital/vflow) - High-performance, scalable and reliable IPFIX, sFlow and Netflow collector. (1149)
* [Wave Terminal](https://waveterm.dev) - Wave is an open-source, AI-native terminal built for seamless developer workflows with inline rendering, a modern UI, and persistent sessions.
* [wellington](https://github.com/wellington/wellington) - Sass project management tool, extends the language with sprite functions (like Compass). (303)
* [woke](https://github.com/get-woke/woke) - Detect non-inclusive language in your source code. (510)
* [yai](https://github.com/ekkinox/yai) - AI powered terminal assistant. (850)
* [zs](https://git.mills.io/prologic/zs) - an extremely minimal static site generator.

## Benchmarks

* [autobench](https://github.com/davecheney/autobench) - Framework to compare the performance between different Go versions. ⭐ 99
* [go-benchmark-app](https://github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app) - Powerful HTTP-benchmark tool mixed with Аb, Wrk, Siege tools. Gathering statistics and various parameters for benchmarks and comparison results. ⭐ 28
* [go-benchmarks](https://github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks) - Few miscellaneous Go microbenchmarks. Compare some language features to alternative approaches. ⭐ 150
* [go-http-routing-benchmark](https://github.com/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark) - Go HTTP request router benchmark and comparison. ⭐ 1667
* [go-json-benchmark](https://github.com/zerosnake0/go-json-benchmark) - Go JSON benchmark. ⭐ 11
* [go-ml-benchmarks](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/go-ml-benchmarks) - benchmarks for machine learning inference in Go. ⭐ 32
* [go-web-framework-benchmark](https://github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark) - Go web framework benchmark. ⭐ 2137
* [go_serialization_benchmarks](https://github.com/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks) - Benchmarks of Go serialization methods. ⭐ 1621
* [gocostmodel](https://github.com/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel) - Benchmarks of common basic operations for the Go language. ⭐ 62
* [golang-benchmarks](https://github.com/SimonWaldherr/golang-benchmarks) - a collection of golang benchmarks. ⭐ 142
* [golang-sql-benchmark](https://github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark) - Collection of benchmarks for popular Go database/SQL utilities.
* [gospeed](https://github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed) - Go micro-benchmarks for calculating the speed of language constructs. ⭐ 126
* [kvbench](https://github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench) - Key/Value database benchmark. ⭐ 26
* [skynet](https://github.com/atemerev/skynet) - Skynet 1M threads microbenchmark. ⭐ 1061
* [speedtest-resize](https://github.com/fawick/speedtest-resize) - Compare various Image resize algorithms for the Go language. ⭐ 245

## E-Books
### E-books for purchase

* [100 Go Mistakes: How to Avoid Them](https://www.manning.com/books/100-go-mistakes-how-to-avoid-them) - 
* [Black Hat Go](https://nostarch.com/blackhatgo) - Go programming for hackers and pentesters.
* [Build an Orchestrator in Go](https://www.manning.com/books/build-an-orchestrator-in-go) - 
* [Continuous Delivery in Go](https://www.manning.com/books/continuous-delivery-in-go) - This practical guide to continuous delivery shows you how to rapidly establish an automated pipeline that will improve your testing, code quality, and final product.
* [Creative DIY Microcontroller Project With TinyGo and WebAssembly](https://www.packtpub.com/product/creative-diy-microcontroller-projects-with-tinygo-and-webassembly/9781800560208) - An introduction into the TinyGo compiler with projects involving Arduino and WebAssembly.
* [Effective Go: Elegant, efficient, and testable code](https://www.manning.com/books/effective-go) - Unlock Go’s unique perspective on program design, and start writing simple, maintainable, and testable Go code.
* [For the Love of Go](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/love) - An introductory book for Go beginners.
* [Go in Practice, Second Edition](https://www.manning.com/books/go-in-practice-second-edition) - Your practical guide on the ins-and-outs of Go development, covering the standard library and the most important tools from Go’s powerful ecosystem.
* [Know Go: Generics](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/generics) - A guide to understanding and using generics in Go.
* [Lets-Go](https://lets-go.alexedwards.net) - A step-by-step guide to creating fast, secure and maintanable web applications with Go.
* [Lets-Go-Further](https://lets-go-further.alexedwards.net) - Advanced patterns for building APIs and web applications in Go.
* [The Power of Go: Tests](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/tests) - A guide to testing in Go.
* [The Power of Go: Tools](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/tools) - A guide to writing command-line tools in Go.
* [Writing A Compiler In Go](https://compilerbook.com) - 
* [Writing An Interpreter In Go](https://interpreterbook.com) - Book that introduces dozens of techniques for writing idiomatic, expressive, and efficient Go code that avoids common pitfalls.

* [Go Faster](https://leanpub.com/gofaster) - This book seeks to shorten your learning curve and help you become a proficient Go programmer, faster.
* [Go Succinctly](https://github.com/thedevsir/gosuccinctly) - in Persian. (23)
* [Go with the domain](https://threedots.tech/go-with-the-domain/) - A book showing how to apply DDD, Clean Architecture, and CQRS by practical refactoring.

* [The Go Developer Roadmap](https://roadmap.sh/golang) - A visual roadmap that new Go developers can follow through to help them learn Go.
